chaūceler reſon rede name ſayenge theſe wordes doughter ſothfaſtnes ſaith ſhe peryſſheth leſeth hyr name man haue deth hath deſerued hyr acordeth hir liſter riȝtwyſnes y• ſyde mercy ſayth ſhe periſſheth leſeth hir name man haue mercy ſaued hir accordeth fourth ſiſter pee wherfor accorde theſe gyder fynal dome mater lete made good deth man ſo y• one founden wyd • utenjudicium • egis ſynne y• may wyl innocētly charyte ſuffre deth mā haue y• aſken may dethe lenger holde hym without ſyn̄e treſpas ſo ſhal perſe hym makynge hym hole wey thorugh whyche man may paſſe ſaued ¶ ſentence dome hyhe hylles depe pytte helle▪ whether ther ony man myght take good innocente dethe none foūden clene ſynne noo child one dare byrthe ſo ſhe went vp hir ſyſters tellynge men hadde forfetid vnable ne enmy ſkylful y• cōqnerd man wycked ſleyȝt fals wyſdome ſo ouercome vaynquyſſhed good ſleyȝte trew wyſdom whan reſon ſayd verditeur fader ſaid wille ſhold ſo ſone yamia et veri • • obuia uerūt ſibi inſciciam et pax fe aſſēt therto holy ghoſt ſaid wold wyrche ther alſo fellē doun al ſpirites heuen ſoueraynly thankyd holy trinyte foure ſiſters forſeid kyſſed made accorde ſo fylfylled yt ꝓphete dauid ſeid mercy ſothfaſtnes metten louely gyder riȝtwyſneſſe pee hauen kyſſed thus termined ended grete coūceyl heuen reſtorynge man ſauacion whiche proceſſe ſhal taken lykenes maner parable deuoute yere ſhe dyde ſhe lyued tyme may knowe rouelacions made hyr deuout woman whiche men trowē ſeint elizabeth y• whiche reuelacions cōteyned amonge lady told ſame woman ſayd thys maner fader moder leften temple purpoſed andnota propo 〈…〉 ſette ſtably herte haue god tader ofte ſythes wyth grete denocion thoughte▪ myght pleſynge god ſo wolde voucheſauf ſende grace herewith taught lernyd lawe lord god whiche lawe heſtes dyddynges▪ pryncypally kepte thre hert ¶ fyrſte 〈…〉 thou ſhalt loue thy lord god thy herte wyth thy ſoule wyth alle thy mynde wyth alle thy myghtes ſecond thou ſhalt loue thy neyghbour thy felf andca iii thyrdde thou ſhalt hate thyne enemy theſe kepte trewely herte anone concyued toke al vertues ben conteyned hem may ſoule haue vertue loue god herte thys loue comethnota odiū inimicoru▪ plente grace hit comen abydeth ſoule renneth oute water hit ſo hate enemyes ſaye vyces ſynnes wherfore wylle haue grace kepe hit hit behoueth diſpoſe ordeyne herte loue hate ſaid ſonota • cionem marie wylle thou doo maner dyd roſe vp algate mydnyghte wente forth aulter temple wyth al grete deſyre wyl affeccion coude myghte aſked grace almyghty god kepe tho thre heſtes byddynges lawe ſo ſtandyngenota ſeptē peticione • marie aulter made ſeuen peticions god ben theſe fyrſte aſked grace god thorugh whiche myȝt fulfylle heſte loue ſaye loue al herte ſecond aſked myght loue neyghbour wyll lykyng wolde make loue loueth thyrdde wold make hate eſchewe al thyng hateth fourth aſked mekenes paciēce begnignite ſwetnes al vertues whych myȝt gracions pleſyng god ſyȝte v peticōn made god wold lete ſee tyme whiche bleſſyd mayden ſhold borne y• ſhold conceyue bere god ſone wold kepe myn eyen myght ſee hir myn eres y• myȝt hir ſpeke tonge myȝt prayſe hir handes myȝt douȝter y• al grace hade wythoute trauayle nay ſo telle wete grace yefte ne vertue god withoute grete trauaylle contynuel prayer ardent deſyre proffūde deuocion wyth many teres mykel afflyccion ſpekynge thynkynge doynge alweye coude myghte pleyſyng god ſaye oute take holy grace thorugh whiche halowed moders wombe ferthermore lady ſayd wete thou wel certayne cometh grace mannes ſoule prayer bodyly affliccion haue yeuen god tho thynges may though ben lytyl fewe cometh y• ſoule bryngyng hym ſo grete ſo hyhe yeftes grace ſemeth ſoule ſhe faylled ſelf leſeth mynde thynketh euer ſhe ſaide god then̄e wente ſhe home ageyne nazareth wryten proceſſe ſtory hyr natiuite thus mykel tyme ſuffyſeth haue mynde cōtemplacion tho thynges befellen incarnacion whiche ſoo wylle wel thynke haue prayer hyr meditacōns perauēture redyng prophecie yſaye touchyng incarnacōn yet alſo ſwyftely flew • ernard lord come fonde holy trimen meſſager thou ſhalt vnderſtonde thys bleſſid incarnacion hyhe werke holy trinite though hit ſo perſone ſone incarnate become man beware thou erre imaginacōn god holy trinite ſuppoſynge theſe thre perſones fader ſone holy ghoſt ben thre erthely men thou feeſt thy bodyli eye whiche ben thre dyuerſe ſubſtaūces eche departed fro ſo none hem nay ſo thys ghoſtly ſubſtūce holy trynyte tho thre perſones ben one ſubſtaūce one god yet ther none theſe perſones yet may thou vnderſtōde man̄es reaſon ne conceyue thy bodyly wytte therfore take generall doctrine mater algate tyme thou hereſt thynkeſt trynyte godhede ghooſtly creature aungels ſoules whiche yu mayſt ſee propre kynde thy bodyly eye ne fele thy bodyly wytte ſtudye fer mater occupye thy wytte therwith thou woldeſt vnderſtōde bodyly reſon wylle whyle thys boiſto • body lyuyng erthe therfore whan thou hereſt ony ſuche thyng byleue paſſeth thi kindely reſon trowe ſoth faſtly ſoth holy chirche techeth goo ferther ſo thou ſhalt bileue thys mater incarnacōn ſecond perſone trynyte goddes ſone henene come erthe tooke fleſſhe blood bleſſyd vyrgyne mary become veray man yet neuer departed fro fader holy ghoſt godhede euer dwelling ſtylle hem one god heuen goo oure purpos incarnacion ſayd take hede haue mynde thou preſent pryue chā • er af lady holy trynyte preſent aungel gabriel lorde hows ſuche gheſtes ben ſuche thynges ben done though holy trynyte euer preſēce god hede neuertheles thou maiſt thynke vnderſtonde ſpecial maner reſon hys hyhe werke incarnacion gabriel entred mary chambre ſtoken fro men fro aungels ſaynt bernard ſayth knelynge wyth reuerence beganne meſſage theſe wordes ſaid heyle ful grace oure lord bleſſyd thou wymen aboue wymen mary herynge meſſage thys newe gretynge ſhe neuer herd aſtonyed abaſſhed nought anſwerde thought gretynge thys myghte abaſſhet troublet ony vycious ſynfull diſtourblynge ne agaſte preſence wonte aungels preſence ſyghte hem goſpel ſayth ſhe aſtonyed worde newe gretynge neuer wonte fore grete maner moche gretynge ſhe ſawe ſelf cōmended prayſed ſpecially thre grete thynges yt ſhe parfyghtely meke ſhe muſt nedes abaſſhed hyhe gretynge ſhe commēded ſhe ſul grace oure lord y• ſhe bleſſyd aboue wym̄en moche parfyȝte meke maye prayſynge withoute abaſſhement ſhamefaſtnes therfore ſhe abaſſhed aſtonyed wyth honeſte ſhamefaſtnes alſo drede though ſhe trowed wel aūgel ſaid ſothe neuertheles ſhe drede word mykel ben parfytely meke haue propirte rewarde owne vertues rather taken hede owne defaultes thorugh mowen • gate profyte vertuouſly holdyng hem ſelf grete vertue lytyl lytyl defaulte grete ſo wyſe ſhamefaſt dredeful ſhe helde pee anſuerd mayſt thou take enſample mary fyrſt loue ſo lytary prayer departyng fro men thou mayſt worthy aungels preſence ferthermore lore wiſdome thou ſpeke kepe ſcylēce loue lytyl ſpeche ful grete proutfytable vertue marye herde firſte aungel twyes ſpeke ſhe wold anſwere one ageyne therfore hit abhominable thyng grete repreef mayden vyrgyne grete iangler namely relygyous ferthermore goſpel aū arte ful grace thy ſelf alſo thou haſt founden ſpeciall grace god recouerd grace al mankynde bernar • loo thou ſhalt cōceyue bere chylde thou ſhalt calle name jheſus betokeneth ſauyour ſhall ſaue fro ſynne dampnacōn al peple trewely hopen hym ¶ ſayth ſaint bernard god graūte lord jheſus voucheſauf nombre amonge peple ſo ſaue fro ſynnes ſothely drede manynot • ſhewen hem peple whiche knoweth ne hath people drede maye ſaye many ſemen peple religyous holy people worſhippeth wyth lyppes ſothely herte ful ferre fro wolt thou knowe thou peple wylt thou people • yt lord jheſus bydeth ye goſpel ende may thou ſay ſaynt bernard 〈…〉 deſyrynge kīgdome jhū thus come lord jeſu putte aweye al ſclaūders • ynne fro thy reame ſoule ſoo thou maye reygne therein oweth couetyſe cometh chalengeth reame me▪ preſumpcyon coueyteth lorde pryde wolde quene lechery ſaith wol regne de traccion enuy wrath glotony ſtryuen whiche hem ſhal pricipally regne mykel wa • e ageynſtonde hem thou lord jheſu deſtroye hem thy vertue take thou thy reame thy kyngdome haue trewe kyng thy lord jheſu whan aungel hadde tolde theſe condicions worthynes bleſſid child •• meke mayden mary choſen mo▪ der ſhe ſpake fyrſte abraham dauyd deſyreden hyr aſſente ſtode ſauacion mankynde alſo aūgel gabriel ſtōdynge reuerence lady enclynyng mylde ſemblaunce abydeth anſwer hys meſage ſyde take hede mary ſtant ſadly drede mekenes grete auyſement hauyng pryde ne veyne glorye al hyhe prayſynge ſaid tho ſouerayne yeftes grace ſhe hath herde yeuen hir neuer yeue creature ſhe aretid grace god lerne yu enſāple hir ſhamefaſte vertuouſly meke withouten theſe two vertues maydē bernar • hede vyrgynyte lytyl worthe saynte bernarde ſaith vyrgynyte fayre vertue mekenes mor neceſſary thou may ſauf wythoute fyrſt withoute mekenes thou maye ſoo moche dar hardly ſaye withoute mekenes vyrgynite mary pleſynge god mary meke ye holy ghoſt reſted vpon hir ſayth ſaynte bernard ye laſt ende goſpel ſeith mylde maydē mary ſhe herde wyſely vnderſtonde aungels wordes good auyſement yaf hir aſſente thys maner writen reuelacōns ſhe knelyd doun ſouerain deuocion holdyng vp bothe hir handes lyftyng vp eyen heuen ſayd theſe wordes loo handmayden ſeruaunt lord▪ done fulfilled thy word ſo theſe meke lowe wordes mary ende thou haſt enſample grete mekenes thou haddeſt hyr ſylence begynnyng loo ſhe choſen godes moder doune thanked god grete yefte mekely beſechynge hym deuoutly prayenge wold ſende hir grace teche hir ſo al come done aboute hys bleſſyd ſone ſhe myght fulfylle hem doo hem wythout defaulte thus mykel touchynge goſpel proceſſe incarnacyon jheſu cryſte ¶ feſte annūciacion tho thynges befelle daye take good hede vnderſtōde worthy thys feſte thys ſolēpnyte haue therfore ghoſtly myrthe make ſpeciall feſte thy ſoule thākynge god inwardly ſuche neuer herd ſōlempnite al holy trynyte fader ſone holy ghooſt whome ſouereyn dede incarnacyon wroughte fulfylled ſaid thys alſo ſpecial feſte oure lady 〈◊◊〉 ſone jheſu took hir vp wyth hym bliſſe worſhpfully crowned hir quene heuen euerlaſtynge hir deſyre loue fulfylled whan ſhe endeleſly thoruȝ plēte charyte knyt hyr bleſſyd ſone jheſu hyr ſo fedde y• bleſſid fruyt ſhe coueyted nomore▪ ſhe thoruȝ fylled al goodnes blyſſe joye outen ende thus ſhortely fyue partyes gretynge aue maria maye vnderſtande v joyes bleſſid mary v vertues ſhe ſoueraynly hem haue ſaid y• whiche gretyng comyn vnderſtō dyng may thus ſaid englyſſhe haile mary ful grace lord bleſſid thou ſoueraynly wymen y• fruyte thy wombe jheſus euer bleſſyd • e yf lyſte thys gretyng worlde folowed bleſſyd moder mayden mary beryng kyngs 〈…〉 heuen jhs wyth hyr one ſyde goth worſhpful wydowe anne wyth grete reuerence vnſpecable joye louynge prayſyng god thys ſolempne worſhipful gruche ne heuy vnkyndneſſe ageynſt god notwithſtondyng joſeph ſo nyhe acceptable god neuertheles appierynges aungels reuelacions done hym openly wakyng maner dremes ſlepynge thyrdde notable thynge haue enſample lord ſuffreth derlynges dyſeaſed thorugh perſecucions tribulacions ſheweth well mary joſeph tyme knewe childe ſought ſlayn myght ſorouful though ſo weretercium tribulacō electorum knewen wyſten wel goddes ſone neuertheles ſenſualite reaſon hem myȝt kyndely ben diſtourbled meued ſay thys maner lord god fader almyghty nede hit thy bleſſid ſone flee thou myȝteſt defende hym fro hys enemyes kepe hym ſauf alſo tribulacion dyſeaſe ſoo moche hem behoueth goo ſoo ferre londe knewe hard weyes noyous ſythen ſoo mykel vndiſpoſed goynge trauayllyng oure lady yongth tendyrnes joſeph y• ſuffreſt trybulacōn kepe theryn pacience loke haue herof pryuelege hym wold take hymquartum benignitas erga nimico • ſelf ne yeue moder fourth notable thynge may cōſydere y• grete benignyte mercy lord myght anone momente haue dyſtroyed enemyes purſueden hym yet wold benygnely ſwetely choſe rather flee yeue ſtede tyme malyce wodeneſſe wycked herode auēgyd myght ryghtwyſly hym profūde mekenes expediente haue hem many ſkylles then̄e lady ſory ſaid ſhe myght fynde hir ſone nyght cloſed hir chā bre toke hir prayer beſt remedy caas ſayeng maner almyghty fader heuen full mercyo ••• io •• • pyte hit lyked yow youre wylle yeue dere ſone loo fader haue loſt hym wote thou knoweſt thynge telle ſhewe ſwete ſone yeue hym agayn good fader take hede beholde ſorowe herte grete necligence knowleche wel haue offendyd caas neuertheles falle ignoraūte ye grete goodnes yeue hym ageyn may lyue withoute hym thou ſwete ſone ihu arte thou arte thou herberowed lord whether thou goon vp heuen ageyne thy fader wote wel thou arte god goddes ſone then̄e woldeſt thou telle alſo wote wel thou arte veray man borne kepte bare ye egypte fro malyce herode ſought ſlee whether ony wycked man hath aſpyed fader heuen almyghty kepe ſhylde fro alle perylle malyce dere ſone telle thou arte may come el thou come foryeue neclygence thys tyme behete ſhal neuer efte befalle befalle wote neuer thou knoweſt arte hope lyf al good withoute maye lyue maner ſuche wordes maye deuoutely ſuppoſe nyghte moder cared prayed hyr dere ſone vpon morowe erly mary joſeph ſoughten hym dyuerſe wayes • • den jheruſalem ferthermore ſoughten hym beſely amonge frendes kynneſmē myȝte hym wherfore moder ſo ſory ſhe myȝte maner comforted thirde daye whan comen jheruſalem ſoughten hym temple foūde hym ſittynge amonge doctoures lawe heryng hem entēty • ly aſkynge hem queſtions wyſely anone oure lady ye ſyȝt hym ſhe gladde ſhe torned tro deth lyf therewith knelynge downe thanked god inwardly wepinge joye alſo ſoone chylde jheſus ſawe moder wente hyr ſhe vnſpekable joye clypped hym armes kyſſynge hym ofte ſythes holdynge hym barme reſted whyle hym tendernes tyll ſhe take ſpyryte thenne ſhe ſpake hym ſayd dere ſone haſt yu done v maner lo thy fader grete ſorowe haue ſoughte al theſe thre dayes then̄e anſwerde ageyn ſaid eyleth ſeche knowe ye wel behoueth occupyed tho thynges longen worſhyp fader theſe wordes vnderſtode yt tyme then̄e ſaid moder sone wylte thou goo home ageyn v mekely anſwerynge ſaid wylle doo ye wylle doo pleaſyng yow ſoo ſubget hem wente home ageyne hem vnto theyr cyte nazareth ¶ thys forſaid proceſſe jheſu hope dyde maner lyued tho thre dayes may ſuppoſe wēte ſomed • 〈◊〉 hoſpytale poore men ſhamefaſtly prayed aſked herborow ete laye wyth poore men poore chylde ſome doctoures ſayen begged thoſe thre dayes therof lytel force ſo folowe hym innota parfyte mekenes vertues beggynge without forth meke herte within forth lytel worth perfeccion ferthermore forſaid proceſſe maye note lerne thre notable thynges v fyrſte wyll perfytely loue god ſhall dwelle amonge fleſſhely frendes kynneſmen muſt leue hem goo fro hem token wherof chylde jheſus lefte owne dere moder tyme wolde yeue entente ghooſtly werkes fader alſo ſoughte amō ge frendes kynneſmen founden tyme ſeconde ledeth ghoſtly lyf wondre moche ne diſcomforte ouer heuely though ſomtyme ſoo drye ſoule voyde deuocion forſake god thys maner befell goddes moder ſaid wherfore diſpeyre ther ſeche beſely jheſu holy medytacions good werkes ſpecially deuoute prayer ſhall fynde hym laſt due tyme thirde man herte ſee god enſample hym goo ſolytary place moche thou mayſt ſauynge thyne aſtate flee cōpany fleſſhely mē seche curioſite newe knowleche frēſhippes fylle thyn eyen thyn eres vayn fantaſyes reſt ſoule flee venemous ſoule ſolitary beyng fleyng bernard 〈…〉 ſay 〈…〉 ▪ ſayth vertuouſly ſoule body ſay yt man entencion deuocion ſpiryte departed fro ye world men ioyned ſo ſpyryte god▪ ſpyryte aſketh ſolytary beynge body maner tyme ſpecially tyme ſpecial prayer alſo tyme hem owen way degree ſolytary recluſe ſome relygious therfore ſaith ſame ſaint yu art amonge many bodyly men thou maiſt ſolytary alone ghoſtly yf thou loue theſe worldly thynges ye comynalte loueth alſo yf thou deſpyſe forſake tho thynge comynly al men deſyrē taken alſo yf thou flee ſtryues debate yf thou fele ſorewe thyn owne harmes haue mynde wronges done ye auengyd el though thou allone ſolytary body thou arte allone ſoule truly ¶ generally manere companye men thou arte cōuerſaūt beware ſpecially thoo thynges yf thou wilte truly ſolytary ſpirite thou curious beſy ſercher menes conuerſacyon▪or el preſumtuouſe temerary demer men ſaynte bernardes ſentence ſolytary beynge whiche may vnderſtāde bodyly ſolicitude ſuttyſeth oute ghoſtly haue ghoſtly bodily helpeth ful moche puttynge away occaſion without forth myȝt drawe ioule within forth fro onynge and▪ knyttynge hir ſpouſe jheſu criſt wherfore maye ſo knytte hym grace aboute wille myght tolowe hym ſaye true ſolitary beynge layde deuoute prayer faſtyng diſcrete bodily penaū ce doyng ferthermore cōuerſacōn deſerte wasnota •• ne amonge y• erthe deuoutely honoured hym ſalued hym theyr lord almyghty god oure lord benyngly ſwettely ok hem vp enclynyng hem hede hit knowlechyng hym ſelf veray man ſomwhat laſſe lowed fro aūgels then̄e thy wyf folowe ſhal bryng better parfyte weddynge thys āone wythoute johan lefte hys wyf folowed jheſus thys forſayd proceſſe may many thynges doctryn edificacion fyrſt lord jheſus wold come preſente ſemynge yaf moder ſayd woman ſaynt bernard ſayth taught v ben relygious haue forſake world beſy haue grete care fleſſhely parentes ſoo theyr nede lette ghoſtly exercyſe long ben worlde ſo longe • dette parentes haue left forſake ſelf mykel free delyuerd y• 〈…〉 beſineſſe hem ſo finde writen ther cam vpon tyme hermite monke forſake worlde lyued ſolytaryly deſerte owen fleſſhely broder prayeng hym hys helpe certeyne nede touchinge world bade hym go hys broder dede longe afore whanne wondred byddynge ſayde dede knewe wel monk anſwerde ſayd ſo washe dede world ſoo thaught v lord jhſus haue therfore paſſe ouer atte tyme ferthermore haue techynge pacience hope dede 〈…〉 lady lefte ſtraunge anſwere ſayd ſoo tyme callen jheſu helpe atte oure nede bodily ghoſtly though finde anone rather geſtes mete holding doune hir face hir eyen erth ſhe letted tyll ſhe come hym ſhe ſought inwardlynō 〈…〉 loued lord jheſu anone then̄e ſhe fell doune grounde proſtrate hys foot wyth grete inward ſorowe ſhame hyr ſynnes ſpake hyr herte hym thynkynge thys manere ſwete lord wote well truly knowleche yt ye god lorde haue offendyd hyghe mageſte many grete offenſes treſpaces ſo mykel knowleche ſothely ſynnes ben wythoute nombre grauell ſee mykel belyue mercy paſſeth alle thynge therfor wretchyd ſynful come flee grete mercy forthynkynge inwardly haue offendid aſkynge mercy foryeuenes behete herte amē dement ſyn̄es ſhall neuer power ſake youre obedyence good lord put fro forſake repentaūce refute wote well may none haue alſo wyll haue loue ſoueraynly aboue alle wherfore gode lorde forſake ye punyſſhe ye youre wille neuertheles aſke algate mercy wyth wyth grete turſte hys mercy inward affectyon hys loue ſhe kyſſede hys feete otfe ſadly wepynge ſhedynge teres ſo thylke ſhweſſhe feete wyth hem ſo ſemeth yt lord jheſus went bare fote whan ſhe wel wepte grete drede hyr vnworthynes hyr here ſholde touche hyr lordes fete ſhe wiped hym deuoutely ſhe borught thing wyth hyr ſo precyous wype alſo ſhe wyped hem wyth hyr heer mendement ſhe beofre treſpaced hyr heer yt ſaye ſhe hadde vſed pryde vanyte ſhe wold put hyt vſe mekenes deuocion alſo feruēte loue deuocion yt ſhe hym ſhe wolde letted therof bi ye fetching ony cloth wipe hem ſo wypyng feete afterwarde de uoutly kiſſynge hem ofth ſythes ſhe āoynted hem precious oynement ſhe brouȝt wyth hyr ſuppoſyng pe rauētur oure lordes feete hard weye alſo inward deuocyon begynnynge wyth drede hys feete ſhe dyd boldenes loue anoynted hys hede lord god ſo wold inwardly thinke take hede dede woman circumſtaūce therof mykel ghoſtly fruyte ſholde fynde theryn ſterynge inward repentaūce ſin ne true loue jheſu grete deuocyon forth proceſſe take hede alſo maner oure lord jheſu thys tyme benygnly pacyently ſuffreth hyr doo hyr wylle lyked hym full welle knowynge inward affection true loue hyr herte ſoo alle tyme ſeaced etyng alſo wyth hym gheſtes wondryng woman vnkouth dede pacyence oure lord jheſu hys ſuffraūce hys feſte ſoo ſhewynge perfection vertues alſo juſtifyeng ſynfull ſtant pryncypally true loue god ſayd symon concluſyon thus many ſyn̄es ben foryeuen hyr ſhe loued myket then̄e tourned hym mawdeleyne ſhold moſte wondringe al gheſtes vpon repreef ſhame yt ſhe ſyn̄e ſo grete withinforth ſhe foryate ſhame reprefe wythoute forth ſo dede ſhe knowleched openly ſynne generall alſo wyll ſpecial refuſinge haue herd reherced openly tolde hym ſhe cam lord jheſu whiche ſhe wiſte well knewe ſpecyall leſte parte therof myght reſonably haue reprehended hir openly hade foryeuen curtois lord ful grace mercy true feyth bilyue whiche grounded parfitely hope charite ſayd made hir ſauf ſo ſhall moſte ſynfull man euer ſhall be▪ yf haue truly grounded herte veray contricion ſhe thenne withoute doubte wyll therin lord grete grace endleſſe goodnes euer redy helpe hele tho aſked hym truely goynge wyth hym towarde hous came worde forſard prynce yt doughter dede therfor̄ bodē hym ye ſhold make mayſter jhūs traueyle vayne trowed well yt might hele ſeke reyſe dede neuertheles lorde jhūs letted myſby leue ne ſcornynge doo grace badde fader ſholde drede on̄ly byleue whā came hous foūde cuſtome many wepyng mournful mynſtralſy aray exequyes ſayd hē wepeth wenche dede ſlepyth then̄e ſcorned vnd er ſtode meaned though ſhe dede hem neuertheles myghte reyſe make lyue ſhe dyde ſlepe then̄e puttynge oute hous ſauf ye tader moder thre apoſtles peter james john lorde jheſus badde wēche ryſe anone ſhe roſe vp fro dethe lyfe ete hool proceſſe goſpell vnd er ſtondyng letter whyche maye ghoſtly vnderſtonde fyrſte lord god thenne reyſed bodily doughter prayer faythe fader ſoo reyſeth oft tymes ghoſtly dede ſoule ſyn̄e lyfe grace thrugh prechynge prayeng holy men fayth holy chyrche lorde jhūs ſpared myſbyleue ſcornyng helpe hym aſked grace ſo ſholde mē ſpare profite ſoules namly men holy chirche ſpare preche goddis worde whan lōgeth offyce reyſing dede ſoules ghoſtly lyf though ſome men ſcorne hem reproue hem therfore ſaynt auguſtyn ſay falleth daye man ghoſtly dede bi ful aſſent herte dedely ſyn̄e prechyng goddes worde compūcte herte therof thorugh grace though herde lorde bydde hym ryſe ſoo reyſed ſoule repentaūce fro dethe lyfe hous yt borne wythoute dede ouer ſyn̄e fyrſt maner dedely ſynne lighteſt ryſe therof thrugh grace betokened fyrſte dede bo dy reyſed jheſu houſe ſayd neuertheles manere dedely ſyn̄e on̄ly aſſent mooſt perillous yf longe abyde ſpecially yf ghoſtly hye pryde enuye ſaynt gregory ſayth ſomtyme greuous ſyn̄e goddes ſyghte pryde delyberacōn herte dede lechery yet aldaye one gretly charged ſaye lechery ſeldom lityll therfore ben many men deceyued paſſe ouer reyſynge ſeconde dede body wryten ye goſpel ſaynt luke tyme lordeof 〈…〉 dede bo 〈…〉 jhūs came cite named naym diſciples wyth hym moche peple mette yate cyte dede body borne bere allone ſone widow came wyth corſe moche folke cytee wyth then̄e lorde hauynge pyte grete ſoro wydowe meued thrugh endles mercy badde yt ſhe ſholde wepe thenne nighyng towchyng bere therwyth beren ſtandinge ſtyll ſpake body thyſe wordes thou yonge man ſaye aryſe vp anone roſe fro dethe lyfe wente fete began ſpeke ſoo betoke moder alyue ye proceſſe goſpel forſayd lorde jhū moche thy mercy ſhewed ſynfull man whiche thou reyſedeſt dede body borne towarde beryeng prayer made on̄ly ſtyrynge thyn endles godenes pyte soo thou reyſeſt daye ghoſtly hem bē dede ſoule grete ſyn̄es fleſſhly ghoſtly yeuyng thy grace oft time thou prayed ſought ony deſerte thrugh whiche ſynfull men ſtyred repentaūce forſakyng ſyn̄e ſoo ſhryfte penaūce doynge lawes holy chirche ben reyſed ghoſtly lyf grace firſt dede ſyn̄e performed dede yf ſoo ſynne openly knowen euyl enſample ſclaūder thenne nede open penaunce holy chirche hath ordeyned lord jhūs yaue enſample open reyſynge forſayd dede body opē ly borne dede y• bere wythout forth y• ſyght peple bvt princypall purpoſe ſpeke y• reyſynge iii dede body ſaye lazar foure dayes dede aſmoche proceſſe ben many fayre grete notable thynges therfore ſhall ſpecyally gader entente make v ymagynacōn preſent bodily conuerſacōn on̄ly wyth lorde jhū dyſcyples alſo wyth bleſſed deuout meyne ſaye martha mary lazar ſpecyally beloued lorde jeſu goſpell wytneſſith fyrſte ſhall vnd er ſtonde haue mynde proceſſe nexte chapyter vpon tyme whan lorde jhūs walked temple ſaye place called ſalamons porche feſte dedicacyon temple jewes camen aboute hym rauyſſhynge wulues wood dogges wyth grete yre gren̄ynge vpon hym ſayeng thiſe maner wordes longe wolt thou make v ſuſpēſe dwere hertes thou arte thou cryſte telle v openly ſayden bi falſe malycyous entent ende yt yf openly knowleged criſte ſaye enoynted kynge then̄e haue taken hym accuſed hym traytoure cezar emperour rome therfore lorde jhūs knowyng fals ymagynacōn tempred wyſly anſuere in̄ocent lambe amonge ſoo many trechours wulues ſobyrly mekely ſayd hem agayne ſpeke ye leue werke doo name fader tho beren wytnes ouer whan ſayd fader alone token vppe ſtones haue ſtoned hym blaſphemer makynge hym ſelf god ferd er whan lorde concluded partye reaſon auctorytees holy wrytt myght ayen ſay notwythſtōdyng reſonable meke anſuere ſoo goodly wordes contynueden encreaſen malyce aſmoche tyme paſſyon yet comen yeue enſāple penaūce▪ yeuynge ſtede woodneſſe withdrewe hym hondes wente wyth diſcyples beyonde jordan y• place john baptyzed fyrſte aboute xviii myle fro jheruſalem dwelled awhile wyth diſcyples tyme ſoone goſpell telleth purpoos lazar broder martha mary ſayde wexed ſore ſike anone y• two ſyſters ſenden worde jeſu forſayd place beyonde jordan ſayenge hym manere loo lorde thou loueſte lazar ſore ſeke ſayden noo aſmoche hē thought y• ſuffiſed hym loued wyſt meaned alſo perauenture knowing y• malyce jewes agaynſt hym deth lityl wolde haue ſtoned hym durſt calle hym hem com̄ytted wyll then̄e jheſus ſayd hem infirmyte dethe prayſyng god goddis ſone glorifyed therby goſpel tellyth yt ſayd thiſe wordes hem ſpecifyeth ſiſters ſenden tyme preſent grete waye fro hym ſayd neuertheles may vnd er ſtonde proceſſe anſuerde hem thyſe wordes meſſager elles ſayd diſcyples bothe mooſt lykely lorde cōforte y• ſyſters whan herde meſſager thiſe wordes jheſus ſayd infirmyte dethe vnd er ſtondyng perauē ture hym y• brod er ſholde deye bodily y• infirmyte diſcomforte hem whan dede beryed vnd er ſtondynge oure lorde meaned gloryous reyſynge folowed trowynge thenne ſholde haue falle neuertheles dyſcomforte ye tyme torned comfort deſired fyrſt wolde haue hym preſerued fro deth helyd infyrmyte oure lorde jhūs thus fallyth oft tymes wyth hem god loueth ben trybulacion diſeaſe lorde god graūteth hem comfort aſkē deſyren ſuffreth hem tyme diſpeyre deſyre whan wyll fulfylleth deſyre better wolde firſte torneth diſcō forte comfort wolde haue ymagined thoughte ferd er proceſſe goſpel oure lorde certifyed ſeke lazar anſuere ſayd dwellled ſtyll forſayd place two dayes af • ſayd diſcyples goo agayne jewery aferde worde ſayden maiſter right jewes wolde haue ſtoned wolte thou goo agayn thyder then̄e jhūs anſuerde agayn ben twelue houres daye ſayth ben ye aferde ſuppoſyng jewes contynuē malyce wete ye well oft tymes houres chaūgen daye ſo ofte man̄es herte purpoos varyeth chaungeth gooſtly meanynge thyſe wordes ſaynt auſtyn expowneth lord vnderſtondyng hymſelf daye twelue diſcyples twelue houres y• daye reprehended myſbileue vnreſonable drede deth wyll wold yeue coūſeyle hym men god dyſcyples mayſter ſeruaūtes lorde feble ſeke hym ſouerayne leche wherfore maner blamyng hem lorde ſayd hem manere ſentē ce twelue houres daye ſo walkyth day offendeth erreth folowe ye yf ye woll erre wyll ye yeue coūſeyle ſythen nede take counſeyle therfore ſythen ſoo daye houres kindly reaſon houres folowē daye daye houres folowe ye yf ye woll offende erre oure lord jhūs knowyng ſpiryte lazar dede ſayd hem lazare oure frende ſlepyth woll goo wake hym reyſe hym fro ſlepe then̄e diſcyples vnderſtondyng fleſſhly tho wordes kyndly ſlepe ſayden▪ syre yf ſlepe token yt ſhall hole ſaaf ſykeneſſe comynly way kynde ſlepe ſeke men token hele folowyng jhūs meaned deth▪ ſoo maye ſee grete homelynes lorde wyth diſcyples maner bourdyng ſpake wyth hē here▪ declaring hem openly ſpake fyrſt myſtly▪ſayd lazar dede gladde therby bileue maye encreced ſtrengthed knowyng • tyme dethe ſoo rather byleuynge goddis ſone ferd er leuynge many wordes goſpell takyng ſemyth moſt notable edyficacōn aft whā lorde jhūs wyth diſciples torned agayn toward bethanye two ſyſters hadden worde comyng martha one wente agaynſt mary ſatte ſtyll home tyll ſhe called forth biddynge jhūs ſoo ſemyth thiſe wordes ſpecyally y• letter tellynge thyſe ii ſyſters martha maria dyuerſly hadden hē anenſt jhū john theuangeliſt meaned ghoſtly dooth place dyuers condicōns longen hem ben thiſe ii aſtates ſaye actyf lyf contēplatyf lyf doubte mary loued jheſus moche ſiſter martha gladde comynge ſory broders dethe feruently deſired lyfe then̄e went ſhe anone wyth ſyſter oute agaynſt ihū fygure enſā ple ben ſtate contēplatyf lyfe ſhal take vpon hem bodily exercyſe dedes mercy goo oute vyſyte ſeke hem ben pryſon tede hūgry clothe naked ſoo forth el preche teche myniſter ſacramentes holynota chirche ſo y• ben called therto bi biddyng auctoryte holy chirche ihūs name ghoſtly mary bodily ſittynge mary home ſayd martha goyng tyme ſhe mette ihū ſhe felle fete ſayd lorde yf thou haddeſt ben brother dede neuertheles wote well ſoo euer yu aſkeſt god god wolle yeue durſte ſaye vtterly ſhe deſyred inwardly ſayeng thus reyſe brod er fro dethe lyfe ſhe wiſt whether expedient brod er ſholde reyſed whether iheſus wyll therfor̄ ſhe ſet wordes diſcretly manere meanyng lorde wote well thou mayſt reyſe hym therfore yf yu wylt ſhall done whether yu wylt cō mytte thy dome preſūpcōn then̄e ſaid ihs yt brod er ſholde ryſe fro deth life ſo general wordes might taken two maners proue bileue fynall reſurreccōn ſpecifyeng whether wolde reyſe hym ye tyme none therfore martha takyng part y• ſhe ſyker byleue ſayd yt ſhe wyſte well ſhold ryſe generall reſurreccōn laſte daye dome ferd er aſkynge lorde whether ſhe bileued ſayd himſelf yt reſurreccōn lyf euerlaſtyng lyf hē byleueden ſothfaſtly hym ſhe anſwerde fynally thus byleue thou art criſte goddis ſone y• art come world man̄es ſauacōn then̄e byddynge ihūs ſhe wente home▪ called mary ſuſter ſcilence ſaye ſoft ſpekyng ſayeng maiſter comen calleth hun anone • roſe vp went loo expreſly alſo tokened ghoſtly longeth contemplatyf lyfe ſaye fyrſte reſte pee ſcylence ſofte ſpeche low de cryenge grete noys worlde vſeth ferd er tyme lorde ihū calleth hym obedyence cure gouernayle offyce prelacy then̄e enſample mary anone ryſe applyenge wyll goddis wyll loue neuer ſoo moche reſte • haue neuer ſomoche ſwete contemplacōn vnd er ſtonde▪ tyme called ſoo vtterly yf wythſtō de ſholde ſyn̄e dedely inobedyence ferd er may ſee proceſſe goſpel ſpecyall loue homlynes lorde ihūs ſoueraynly mary abode ſtylle martha mette fyrſte wyth hym wolde doo reyſynge lazar vnto tyme mary comen then̄e whan ſhe comen fallen downe atte ihūs fete wyth ſore wepynge teeres ſayd ſhe dide yf brod er dede lorde ihūs ſeenge wepyng y• loued ſoo ſpecyally alſo jewes wepyng ye comen yt tyme cōforte mary wept alſo iii cauſes firſt y• loue y• mary ſpecyally ſyſter lazar alſo ton • b • ſhewe greuouſyte ſyn̄e cuſtome ghoſtly dethe thrugh▪ tokened lazar foure dayes dede beried thirde myſbileue hem whiche byleued hymſelf y• two tymes wroth grutching ſpiryte reyſed lazar vnd er ſtōde ſyn̄e cuſtome oft ſayd yeuynge enſāple ſaynt auſtyn ſaythaug thou arte ouerlayd wyth heuy ſtone dedely ſyn̄e wroth grutche ſpiryte trouble thyſelf maner deminge thyſelf gilty thynke ofte yu haſt ſinned worthy euerlaſting dethe god endles mercy hathe ſpared ſuffred ofte yu haſte herde goſpell forbedynge ſyn̄e thou haſt taken noo rewarde art contynuelly cōtrary fals thy fyrſt baptyſme then̄e ſo thynkynge wyth cōpun • cōn thy ſyn̄e▪ maner aſkyng thy hert ſhall doo whyd er ſhall goo maner ſhall eſcape grete ſyn̄e dredfull peryll euerlaſtyng dethe whan thou ſayſt thus thin herte then̄e cryſt grutchith fayth grutcheth yf fayth v then̄e cryſt v ſo maner grutching hope vpriſyng wepyng trowblyng proceſſe y• goſpel telleth lord ihūs aſked put lazar vnknowing ſpekyng maner man token ghoſtly ſtraūgnes grace hem ben ouerlayed wyth dedely ſyn̄e tyme neuertheles hath alwaye cō paſſyon ſynful mercy redy y• woll truly aſke aſked putt hym ſayden ayen lorde come ſee then̄e wept y• jewes y• ſayden▪ loo loued hym ſo ſhewed affeccōn yt hath ſynfull ſayth y• goſpel came calle rightwis ſyn̄ers penaū ce goo y• graue lazar folowyng lord ihū wyth meyne ſaye two ſyſters martha mary apoſtles jewes many yt tyme comforte ſyſters oure lorde wolde ſee bere wytneſſe ſolempne worthy myracle ſo maye ſee deuoute ymagynacōn lorde ihūs gooth bytwene ii ſiſters talking homly wyth hem wyth hym ſhewyng hym grete dyſcōfort ſorow hadden broders deth ſpecially aſmoche durſt bydde hym come helpe hem kepe fro de drede malice jewes knewe cōſpired dethe hyely cōforted thē ne preſence neuertheles therwyth grete drede hym cauſe jewes then̄e lord benyngly cōforted hem bad hem drede al ſholde beſt faders wyll ſo talkinge togyder camen graue couered wyth grete ſtone aboue then̄e bad lorde ihūs ſholde take awaye ſtone abaſſhed grete tend er loue hym dredynge horribylyte ſtyuke carayne ſholde ought fēde hym ſayden▪ lorde ſtynketh iiii dayes dede ſhewynge therby none hope liuynge ayen lorde ayenwarde cōforted byleue makyng ſtone taken awaye afterwarde liftynge vp eyen heuen ſayd fader thanke thou herdeſt ſothly wote well thou hereſt euer ſaye peple ſtant y• byleue thou haſte ſente whan ſayd thus cryed wyth grete voys lazar come oute thy graue lorde ihū nede crye sothly ſaynt auſtin ſayth ſhew ghoſtly vnd er ſtōding harde toauguſti▪ hym reyſe lyfe ſoule ouerlayed ſtone dedely ſynne cuſtome many ben ſayth ſaynt auſtyn peple whiche ben ouerlayed wyth heuy burden wycked cuſtome perauc̄ture ſome beren ben ouercome wyth lechery gloteny appoſtle forbedeth hem ſayth thus wyll ye dronken wyth wyne whiche lechery ſayenge againnolite ī briari vi may ſoo forth grete myſdedes wyckydnes god forbedeth holy chirche whan ſayd hem dooth none thyſe leeſt ye peryſſh anſuerynge ſayeng maye leue cuſtome lorde jhū reyſe thiſe folke thou reyſedeſt lazar thou arte ſothly reſurreccōn vpriſyng lyfe heuily ſtone wicked cuſtome ouerlayeth men degree on̄ly lered lewde ſeculers alſo religyous nyghe aſtates ſoo woll ſpeken ayenſt wycked cuſtomes ſhall know ſothly experyence noo remedye on̄ly jhū lorde jhū crye thiſe men hye voys yt ſaye ſhewe thy myȝte teyſe hem lyfe grace puttynge away heuy ſtone wycked cuſtome thou reyſedeſt lazar thi crye thy biddyng roſe vp wente graue yet boūden hondes fete tyll loſed vnboū den thy diſcyples thy byddynge grete wonder ſaynt auguſtyn ſayth many men myghte goo graue wyth fete boūden moche wonder roſe fro dethe lyfe foure dayes dede beryed wyth body ſtynkynge careyne tokenyth ſayth ſaynt auguſtyn sothly tokenith whan thou dooſt grete ſyn̄e bi contēpt thou arte ghoſtly dede yf thou contynueſt cuſtomably therin then̄e arte thou dede beried whan yu forthinkeſt within forth ſhryueſt knowlegeſt thy ſynne wythout fourth thenne ryſeſt thou gooſt thy graue nought elles ſaye goo forth ſhewe make knowen outwarde preuy wythin forth knowynge ſhewynge ſyn̄e makyth on̄ly god cryenge wyth grete voys ſaye wyth grete grace callynge butn yet though dede reyſed goone oute graue neuertheles dwelled boūden ſay gylty tyme loſed vnboūden goddis mynyſtres on̄ly gaaf power ſayenge thus hem al ye vnbynde erth ſhal vnboūden heuen al thisn ſayth ſaynt auguſtyn ſentence whiche maye ſee openly ſuffycient auctoryte agaynſt hem reprouen confeſſion ordeyned holy chyrche alſo aſſoylyng curate ſayenge falſly ynough generally euery man ſhryue hym on̄ly herte god preſtes curate holy chirche haue nomore power aſſoyle ſinnes nother man god allonly aſſoyleth none name leuyng fals opynyons gob ynge ende forſayd proceſſe tyme lazar reyſed lif lord jhūs ſayd vnboūden diſcyples ſyſters wyth grete joye lowely thanked jhūs ſouereyn bienfete laddē home wyth hem hous forn ſauacōn mankynde ſoo haue open enſāple y• wycked men reproued god hauen ſomtyme yefte prophecie ſo comyu aſſent thoſe fals prince phariſees counſeyle vtterly ordeyned ſlee innocent lambe jhū ende leeſt peple ſholde byleue tro hym then̄e romayns ſettynge lawe noughte ſholde come deſtroye bothe temple peple▪ fooles foly coūſeyle haue ye wryten wyſe man yt noo wyſdome ne counſeyle agaynſt god therforꝓ • erbio rū 〈◊〉 ſhall fall contrary maner wycked entent perfourmed dede ye ſlewen jhū leeſt romayns ſholde deſtroye place peple befell▪ agaynwarde ye ſlewē jhū place peple • ſtroyed romayns ſtory telleth y• deſtruccō • jhrlm tyte vaſpaſyane ſame manere falleth te tymes worldes wyſdome contrary wiſdome god ofte tymes lorde god torneth beſte worlde demeth worſt ſpecyally enuye grounded entente worldes wyſdome ſhewed openly notable enſample joſeph bretherne enuye worldes wyſdome ſolden egypte vndoynge wolde worſhypp̄ hym ſweuen torned contrary effecte god dis grace ſhewynge hym occaſyon cauſe highe auaūcynge lowe ſubmyſſion hym worſhyppinge ſoo fallyth daye men maye ſee proued experyence wordes chaunged leuynge matere tournyng pourpoos ſayd fals enuyous councelynge due time come y• whiche wold bi freefortitu wyll offer paſſion ſtrongly myghtly ſuffre malyce purſewers vttereſt ende y• harde deth thus alſo vſed tēperaūce nother tyme tyme fledde eſchewinge worldes worſhyp whan peple wolde haue made hym kyng ayen warde vſed ryȝt wyſneſſe whā wolde worſhypped kynge foloweth herafter tyme peple camen ayenſt hym wyth braūches tree manere grete reuerence dooynge hym cyte jhrlm ferd er ſoueraynly vſed rightwyſnes whan entred temple ſharply reproued couetyſe preſtes lawe pharyſees wyth ſcorge droue biars ſellars goddis temple ſoo vſed lorde vertues thiſe foure pryncypall vertues ſaye prudence temperaunce strēgth rightwiſnes doctrine informacōn wher fore ſhall ſuppoſed demed varyaunt conſtaūte ſhall none vſeth thiſe forſayd vertues diſcrecōn dyuers cauſes aſken leuyng mater whā lorde jhūs ſayd offre paſſion tyme ordeyned befor̄ world cam̄ n agayn bethany ſaye ſabbot next palm ſonday whiche place nighe jhrlm aboute ſpace two myle made hym ſupper true byloued frendes full gladde agayn comyng hous symond leproſe name ſomtyme leproſe tyme heled lorde ſupper thiſe homely gheſtes wyth jhū ſaye lazar martha mary hir ſyſter john noteth ſpecyally martha ſerued lazar ſatte borde wyth ſeten alſo wyth lorde mary full brennynge loue jhū taughte wythinforth holy ghoſt toke full precious oynemente ſhedde vpon hede alſo enoyntynge fete whiche precyous oynement ſwete ſauoure fylled al house lete v abide awhile take hede inn wardly forſaid notable pointes firſt lorde jhūs wolde haue ſupper ſpecyally hous forſayd ſymond phariſee ſayd who hous ſelf mary enoynted hym wyth precyous oynement wyth inwarde ſorowe bytter teres cō trycōn perfitly wyth vnſpekable joy ful ſwete teres deuocōn knewe well lorde one ſkylle choſe place tyme loue jheſu alſo wolde haue ſouper symonds hous knowinge charyte true affeccōn cōtynued hym dyſcyples notwythſtondynge frendly reprehenſyon befor̄ bycauſe mary alſo open wytneſſe ye tru reyſynge lazar ete dranke dide hous pharyſee openly preſence many jewes camē tyme ſee on̄ly hymſelf jhū bnt alſo lazar john ſpecyally tellyth ſo maye ſee ſupper hous thife foure perſones dooyng lorde jeſu true ſeruyce dyuers maners ſay mayſter hous charytable hoſpytalyte lazar opē wytneſſe true god bede martha beſy mynyſtrynge longeth true actyf lyfe mary feruent loue deuoute worſhyppyng longeth hye contēplatyf lyf ſyde maye ſee contrary maner yeuynge occaſyon offence lorde jhū enuye fals couetyſe wrōgful demynge enuyous juda colour fals couetyſe grutchynge leſynge ſomoche money ſpēden precyous oynement pretended ſpecyally releuynge poore men therby ſayd yt myghte better haue ſolde thre hūdred pen yeuē hem neden alſo meued wordes otherwyſe good entent ſe mith poore men grutched gretly ſtyred agaynſt mary ſoo grete loſſe precyous oynemente ſhe kepyng ſcylēce lorde anſuerde dyde two tymes reprehēdyng hem declaryng good dede euer mynde enoyntynge befor̄ body beryenge foloweth lorde jhū ſorowfull diſcōfortynge worde ſoo openly declareth thy dethe mary ſpecyally true frendes ſoueraynly thy bleſſid moder maye ſothly byleue worde perced hert ſharply ony ſwerde ſo then̄e al y• myrthe feſte torned ſorowe namly aſmoche knewen jewes vtterly conſpyred dethe neuertheles fals traytour juda cōtynued enuyous indignacōn herof toke occaſion betraey hym ſelle hym dyde weneſdaye next forn xxx pen wherof ſhall ſpeke herafter may ferd er note ſpecially porpoſe iudas parte reprehenden almeſdedes offringes deuocōns people done holy chirche holdynge ſuche yeftes deuocyon foly ſayenge nedfull better yeuen poore men juda thou pretendeſte wyth thy mouth releuynge poore men ſothly entent thy herte groūded enuy ayenſt men holy chirche perteyneth poore men▪ rather thyne owne fals couetyſe excuſacōn thy nyhgonrren 〈…〉 haſt deuocōn nought woll yeue thyn owne good experyence openly techeth comynly ſuche juda felowes ben coueytous ony ſhall fynde ſothly dede ſoo hath doo wyth hē one maner reden goſpel lord jeſu dyuers place ſpecially herafter ayenſt paſſyon reprehēded ſharply ſcrybes pharyſees te tymes namly couetyſe fynde therfore euer bad ye peple wythdraw eyther dymes offrynges yeftes deuocōn done hem ayēwarde bad hē alwaye doo dewte lawe cōmended free deuocōn offrynges opēly ſhewed y• goſpel marke luke whā lord jhūs behelde riche mē put heryeftes offrynges y• tēple arche y• called treſory coufre hauinge hole aboue maner ſtockes y• ben vſed chirches whiche arche called ga • ophilaciū amonge hem ſawe poore wydowe offrynge two mynutes fourth parte ſycle ſubſtauuce lyuelode then̄e lorde reprehendyng one rather cōmendyng ſoueraynly prayſed poor wydowe grete deuocōn ſayd y• lityll yef te goddis ſighte paſſed ye grete yeftes ryche men maye ſee yf take gode hede ye circuſtances y• bi on̄ly proceſſe ſentēce lorde jhūs iudas felowes ben ſufficyently reproued confoūded fals opynyon doctryne ſayd ayenſte holy chirche leuyng proceſſe torne ayen bethanye ymaginynge lorde jhūs forſayd ſupper hous ſi monde went wyth lazar ſyſters hous whyche comyn hoſtrye namly tho fewe dayes folowyn ge paſſyon ete dayes ſlept nygh te wyth diſcyples bleſſed mod er wyth ſiſters worſhipped ſoueraynly worthy ſpecyally mawdeleyne y• wolde neuer departe fro then̄e amonge thoſe true frendes lorde ſayd ſholde tomoche abaſſhed diſtourbled vncouth de de come tolde hem wold morowe goo openly jhrlm then̄e ſoueraynly aferde prayden hym hertly mod er alſo namely wolde put hymſelfe ſoo vtterly enmyes hondes ſothly ferd er dethe conſpyred wythout faylle agaynſt hym y• jewes lorde god cōfortyng hem againward badde hem drede nought ſayd faders wyll take journeye ſhall kepe v ſoo ordeyne v tyme yt ye ſhall ſee amonge al myn enmyes gretteſt worſhyp euer ye ſawe ſhall haue noo power agaynſt haue done wyll tomorowe att euen ſhall come hyder ſauf ſounde thenne thorugh thyſe wordes well comforted neuertheles alwaye dredynge lorde jhūs tame jheruſalem vpon palmſonday caplm xxxvii ſondaye erly vpon morow lorde jheſus dyſpoſed hym ſayd goo jheruſalem new maner vncouthe wyſe euer dyde fulfyll y• prophecye zacarye y• prophete▪ ſayd pourpoos whan lytill bleſſid cōpany cam̄ place middes y• way called bethfage ſente two diſcyples jheruſalem badde hem bryng aſſe fole te • ed comyn waye ordeyned ſerue poore men nede none beſtes owne whan broughte diſcyples layed clothes vpon hem lorde mekely ſette hym firſte lityl vpon aſſe fole ridynge ſymple araye toke way forth jhrlm lorde ſyghte ſee y• kinge kyngis lorde worlde ride ſuche araye namly ſolempne cytee jheruſalem ſothly thou dydeſt thyn dedes enformacōn en ſample may ſee vnderſtonde maner worldes worſhippe takynge thou diſpiſeſt fully pō pe vayne worldes worſhyp hauyuge ſtede golden har ney curyous ſadels bridels ſymple clothes hem ꝓyn helters whan people herde comynge cauſe grete myracle publiſſhed reyſinge lazar wēten ayenſt hym receyueden kynge wyth ympnes ſonges grete joyes makyth mynde lorde wepte notably thre tymes one tyme theprimo dethe lazar wretchydnes mankynde wherby neded deth fyrſte ſyn̄e nother tyme wepte thesecūdo ghoſtly blyndenes vncūnynge man tyme hem dwellen cyte jheruſalem wolden knowe tyme gracyous viſytacōn therfor̄ come cyte vtter diſtruccōn thir de tyme wepte grete treſpaas malyce man andtercio tyme paſſion hangyng croſſe ſawe paſſyon ſufficyent redempcōn men neuertheles toke effecte profyte reproued harde hertes obſtynate doo pena unce woll forthynke amende hem ſyn̄es wepinge ſpekith appoſtle poul whan ſayth jhūs tyme paſſyon wyth grete crye wepynge teres herde fader reuerence thyſe thre wepyng tymes holy wrytte ſpekyth alſo holy chirchequart makith mynde wepte fourth tyme yt whan yonge chylde wepynge hyde fro deuilles myſterye jncarnacōn beholde lorde jhūs ſoo wepynge feynyngly effectuelly largely wyth ſorowfull herte ſpecyally dampnacōn without ende deſtruccōn tem porell hem cytee maye ſothfaſtly trowe dere moder company ſeenge hym wepyng ſoo myght conteyne hem fro wepyng tyme nomore ſholde ſene loſſe ſoules thꝰ lord jeſus rydynge aſſe hauynge ſtede prynces erles boron poore ſymple diſcyples aboute hym anſuerynge diſceyuable queſtions many ſubtill temptynges ſoo occupied fro morowe vnto euentyde whan went wyth diſcyples reſt homly hoſtrye wyth lazar ſyſters bethanye ſayd aſmoche longe proceſſe trete ſpecyall tho mater tyme bytwene lorde jhūs jewes lettynge fro ye purpoos bē paſſyon therfore paſſinge ouer parable enſamples whiche lorde reprehēded jewes proceſſe tyme ſpe ſyall maye generall conſyder note yt one ſyde prynces phariſees ſeenge fauour people jhū therfore dredynge perfourme malyce agaynſte hym openly caſten ſothly fully take hym worde eyther ayenſt lawe▪ elles ayenſt trybute payed emperour rome wherby mighten accuſe worthy dethe lorde preuyte mannes herte open knowyng ſubtylte malyce hem anſuerde wyſely queſtyons ſoo couertly trou ſette wordes ſufficyētly anſwerde yet myghten haue entent ony part laſte ſo confoūded durſt nomore aſke oni queſtyon hym thenne lorde jhūs ſharply reprehended pride ypocryſy couetyſe wyckyd condycōns hem ſpecyally ſcrybes phariſees ſa yenge hem thiſe wordes woo ſcrybes phariſees louen worldly worſhippes many maners ſoo fourth vyces neuertheles badde therwyth peple ſholde kepe fulfyll techynges ſholde folowe werkes euyll liuyng laſt reherſynge vnkyndneſſe jewes ayēſt god generall name cyte jhrlm aſmoche ſoo ofte beſi gader hem togider hen̄e dooth chikens y• way ſauacōn wolde therfor̄ tellyng hem deſtruccōn folowynge temporell euerlaſtynge lefte hem wythdrue hym tēple wyth dyſ ciples many jewes byleued went y• moūt olyuete taught hē ouer enſāples ſhold diſpoſe hem make hem redy laſt ende fynally tolde hē daye dome y• whiche good men y• ſholde befoūden right half god ſholde haue euerlaſtynge lyfe wycked men lyft hō de euerlaſtyng ſorow endles deth thꝰ made lord jhūs ende open prechyng jewes tewiſday towarde euen preuyte ſayd diſciples wete ye well thiſe two dayes paſch ſhall made▪ mannes ſone ſhal bitrayed crucifyed ſorouful worde true diſcyples fals traytour juda full gladde therof thynkynge anone inſtygacōn ſathanas entred herte myghte occaſion dethe fulfyll fals couetiſe herupō ſlepte anone morowe y• weneſday whan ye prynces preſtes wyth ald er men ſcrybes werentradicio •• fe • qua • ta gadred cayphas hous biſſhop toke counſeyle thei myghte ſleyghte take jhūs ſlee hym feeſt daye drede peple juda aſpyenge knowinge coūſeyle went hem profered take hym hem wyll ſoo wolde mede hym doo hym gladde profer graūted ordeined pare hym thyrty grete pen whiche euery peny worth ten comyn pen oure grote worthe foure comyn pen ſoo falſhede couetyſe malyce trechery accorded deth innocentes then̄e fals traytour couetous deſyre pryce forſayd oynement grutched loſte ſay thre hū dred pen fro ye tyme ſought oportunyte miyght bytraye jhū wythout preſence peple forquare ie iunatur feria iiii expreſſe goſpel ſoth yt went jhrlm ne apered openly jewes daye trowe then̄e dyde al day thinke reſonably trowed yt was▪ then̄e mooſt part occupied prayer performynge redempcōn mankynde came fore on̄ly frēdes trowed loued hym alſo cruel enmyes fulfillyng ye pefeccōn charytee taughte diſcyples prayer enmyes hem ſhal purſewe hem ther wyth knowynge ſeenge ſpiryte forſayd malyce da traytour iewes day vtterly caſt ayēſt deth ſoo ſkylfully men may ſuppoſe prayer fader ſpecially ſayd pſalme deus laudem dauyd ſayd prophecye hym juda enmyes longe tyme then̄e mooſt properly ſayd hymſelf time came whiche lord jhūs diſpoſed endeles mercy ſuffre dethe man ſhede precyous blode redempcōn lyked firſt make ſupper diſciples mynde euer laſtynge grete loue hem mankynde fulfill fygure olde homly famylyer wyth lorde jhū ſily went fro ſee neded ordeyned done came hym ſayd syre ye may go ſupper whā ye woll thynges ben redy thenne anone lorde wyth twelue apoſtles wente vppe johan algate terneſſe therfore wepten ſore wythout remedye lo hanged lorde croſſe dede grete multytude gooth awaye towarde cyte ſoroufull mod er wyth iiii ſyſters felawes ſette doune beſyde croſſe beholdeth pyteouſly dere ſone ſoo ferde wyth abideth helpe fro god ſhe myght haue hym bene hym then̄e alſo yf thou beholde well thy lorde thou mayſte haue matere ynough hyghe cōpaſſyon ſeenge hym ſo tormented y• fro ſole fote higheſt parte hede noo hole place ne mēbre wythout paſſion pyteous ſyght joyeful ſyghte pyteous ſighte hym harde paſſion ſuffred ſauacōn likynge ſyghte v matere theffecte haue therby redempcōn sothly ſighte lorde hangynge ſoo croſſe deuout ymagynacyon ſoule ſoo lykynge ſomme creature longe exercyſe ſorowfull compaſſion felen ſomtyme ſoo grete lykyng on̄ly ſoule alſo body y• telle maye noo man knowe alonly experyence felyth thenne may hemichi autē abſit glori ari well ſaye wyth appoſtle betyde neuer joyefull croſſe lorde jhū cryſte amen ¶ tho thynges befell deth lorde jhū none eplm xlv time worſhipful moder lord jheſuca xlv b n ſayd next abode dwellyd beſyde ye croſſe wyth true louers hym named beholdynge lord jheſu contynuelly ſo pytouſly hangynge dede croſſe betwene two theues lo then̄e come many armed men oute cyte toward hem whyche ſente breke legges hem crucyfyed ſo ſlee hem alle oute burye hem cauſe bodyes ſhold abide hangynge croſſe ſabotte day then̄e roſe vp lady alle wyth hyr beſyly loked ſawe hem come wote wherfore fallē grete ſorowe drede namely lady ſpekynge hir ſone thys maner dere ſone maye cauſe al theſe armed men comen agayene wyl doo haue ſlayne dere ſone hadde hoped ben fylled wyth haue done ſemeth yet purſuen dede wote maye doo maye helpe myghte delyuer fro dethe ſhal abide ſee praye thy fader make hem ſofte eaſy ther wyth alle fyue yeden ſtoden byfore croſſe oure lorde then̄e come forſayd armed men hem grete wodenes noyſe ſeenge theues yet lyuyng wyth grete ire hewen breken deſpytouſly legges ſo ſlewē hem caſtē hem anone ſome diche beſyde torned hem agayne camen towarde oure lorde jhū wherfore lady dredynge leeſt wolde doo ſame maner ſone thrugh ſmyten wyth ſorowe herte within forth ſhe cowde nought elles goo beſte armure ſaye kyndly mekeneſſe knelyng doune hem ſpredyng hōdes wyth hygh voys wepyng chere ſhe ſpake hem maner good bred er n beſeche almyghty goddis loue ye torment nomore dere ſone ſothly moſt ſorouful moder ye knowe wel brethern neuer offended dyde ony wronge though ſoo ſone ſemed contraryous ye haue ſlayne hym foryeue wronge offence ye dethe ſone wherfore dooth mercy ye breke ye haue done theues ſoo maye berye body hole nedith ſythen ye ſeen fully dede longe tyme paſſed therwyth john magdalene ſyſters knelynge wyth lady beſoughten ſame wyth ſore wepynge lady doo ye ye lowen fete hem ben mooſt wycked prayen hem haue noo rewarde ony good prayer suppoſe ye bowe pyte hem ben mooſt cruell mooſt wycked wythout pyte ouercome hem ben alder proudeſt mekenes naye proude men haue abhomynacōn mekenes ye traueyllen vayne therwyth one named longius tyme wycked proude true lyuer marter deſpiſyng wepyng prayer wyth ſharpe ſpere openyd ſyde oure lorde jheſu made grete wounde whiche anone ran̄e togyd er bothe bloode water therwyth lady felle doune ſwounyug half dede bytwene harmes magdalene john mowynge bere grete ſorow toke hym man̄es hert riſyng ayenſt hem ſayd ye wycked mē doo ye cruelte see ye dede woll ye alſo ſlaye woman moder go way ſhall berye hym therwyth god wolde wente waye then̄e lady excyted ſo roſe fro ſlepe aſkynge done ſone ſayd none newe thynge ayenſt hym ſhe caughte ſpiryte behelde ſone ſoo greuouſly wounded alſo woūded herte wyth newe woūde ſorow seeſt thou oft time lady day dede ſothly oft ſhe ſawe done ayēſt ſone oni payne wherfore fulfylled ſymeon ſayd prophecyengt • ā ipſiꝰ • ptrāſibit glad • ꝰ longe ſuerde ſhal perce thrugh thyn oune ſoule ſaye ſuerde paſſōn ſorowe befelle oft tymes daye ſothly ſuerde ſpere hath perced body ſone ſoule mod er ſaten doune beſyde croſſe ſhall doo wote may take un body berye cauſe haue neyther ſtrēgthe inſtrumentes apte therfore goo awaye fro hym ſoo hangynge dare longe abyde may not▪ cauſe nyghte come hem mayſt thou ſee ſorow perplexyte ben benygne lorde jheſu ye ſuffre dere moder choſen myrrour worlde youre ſpecyall reſtynge place ſoo tormēted troubled vnneth ſhe hathe ony ſpiryte lyue tyme ſhe ſome manere reſte relecynge ſorowe ¶ takynge doune croſſe lordes body jheſu euenſonge tyme caplm xlvi mene tyme oure lady johan ſayd ſoo grete perplexyte deſolacion ſayd lokeden toward cyte oftymes dyden drede thenne ſee many comynge towarde hem waye whyche joſeph armathre nycodeme bryngynge wyth hem dyuerſe inſtrumentes wyth whyche ſholde take doune body jhū fro croſſe alſo broughte hondred poū de myrre aloe anoynte body ſoo burye hyt then̄e ryſen vp wyth grete drede knowynge wold lord god grete thy ſorowe daye then̄e johan taking hede hem ſo coming ſayd lady sothely ſee comyng joſeph nichodeme then̄e lady caughte ſpiryte gretely comforted ſayd bleſſed oure lord god hath ſente v helpe oure nede hath mynde oure ſorowe hath forſake v oure trybulacyon good ſone johan goo agaynſt hem welcome hem wote well come ſocoure anone johan wente agaynſte hem metten clipped wyth wepynge teres myghte ſpeke grete whyle tendernes cō paſſyon ſorowe hadde walked forth lytyll whyle drawen nyghe towarde croſſe joſeph aſked wythe lady ſtode wyth ye dyſcyples johan anſwerynge tolde hem whoo wyth lady diſcyples coude tell ſayd none hem ſene y• day▪ ferthermore aſkynge tolde done agaynſt lord proceſſe paſſyon come nygh place knelynge doune wepynge honoured lorde jheſu metynge togyder lady ſyſters mawdleyne receyued hem worſhipfully knelyng low bowynge therthe ayen warde knelynge worſhip pynge wyth grete wepynge ſtoden ſoo togyder grete whyle ſpeken laſt lady began ſpeke hem ſaid sothly frendes ye hane done wel ye haue mynde ſo mayſter loued well knowlege plainly ſemyd newe light ryſen comynge wyſte myighte doo therfore god quyte ſayden ayēwarde ben ſory wyth herte thyſe wronges malice done ayenſt hym ſeen well wycked men hauen mayſtry ayenſt ryghtwyſman wolde full gladly haue delyuerde fro ſo grete jniury yf mighte▪ leeſt ſhal ſeruyce lorde maiſter ben come fore then̄e made hem redy take hym downe take good hede maner haue ſayd maner takynge downe ſette ii laders ſydes croſſe one ayenſt another joſeph gooth vpon ladder ſtōdynge yt houde right halfe beſteth hym drawe nayle yt honde full harde nayle grete longe harde driuen ye tree wythout grete thirſtyng doune lordes hōde may done noo force lorde knowyth doyth al truly good entent therfore acceptith dede whan nayle drawen iohn makith ſygne nychode take hym priuely ſoo lady ſee dyſcomfortynge ſame manere nychodeme drawyth oute nayle lyfte honde takyth pryuely johan thenne nychodeme comyth doune draw thirde nayle fete meane tyme joſeph ſuſteyneth body soothly well hym maye ſuſteyne clyppe holyeſt body lorde jheſu therwyth lady takyth hondes reuerently oure lordes ryght hōde beholdeth layeth eyen deuoutly kiſſith ſore wepyng ſighinge whā nayle fete drawē joſeph came ſoftly al layden honde token lordes body layed doune vpon therthe lady toke ye hede ſholders layed arme mawdaleyn redy take kiſſe fete ye whiche ſhe foūde ſomoche grace lyf cōpany ſtoden aboute beholding al makyng grete lamentacōn vpō hym prophecye yt then̄e fulfylled ſayeng yt thei ſhold make ſorowe vpon hym vpon one begeten chylde namly bleſſed mod er al tymes ſore wepyng then̄ ſoroufuly beholdynge woūdes hondes fete ſpecyally ye horryble woūde ſyde takynge hede one another ſeēge hede ſo foule ferde wyth bere drawē wyth ye ſharpe thornes louely face defouled wyth ſpittynges blode here berde drawen awaye fro chekes prophete yſaye ſpekyth perſone thꝰ yaaf blode hem ſmytten chekes hem drewen awaye ¶ beryenge lorde jheſu complyn tyme caplm xlvii lityll whyle lyenge body lorde jheſu bytwene moders armes ſayde whan drewe towarde nyghte joſeph prayed lady ſhe wolde ſuffre body dreſſed manere jewes beryed ſhe looth therto ſayd good bredern take ſoo ſoone childe fro rather berieth wyth then̄e ſayd john dere moder lete v aſſent joſeph nychomede ſuffre oure lordes body beryed elles occaſyon tomoche taryenge ye myght falle lyghtly dangeour ſclaūder ye jewes att ſuggeſtyon john lady wyſe diſcrete thynkynge yt ſhe cōmytted lorde wolde noo lenger lette beryenge▪ bleſſed body lete hem dreſſe wolde john nichodeme joſeph began enoynt body wrappe lynnen clothe manere jewes beryenge neth eles lady kept alwaye hede lappe dreſſe herſelfe mawdleyne fete whā dreſſed legges camen nygh ye fete mawdleyne ſayd praye ſuffre dreſſe fete whiche fonde ſomoche grace ſuffryng aſkyng ſhe helde fete loked vpon hem weping almoſt fayling ſorowe right ſhe lyf wyſſh hē wyth teres cōpunccōn moche ſhe waſſhyth hē wyth teeres grete ſorowe inwarde cōpaſſion ſothfaſtneſſe witneſſith ſhe moche loued therfore ſhe wept moche namly laſt ſeruice doyng mayſter lorde ſoo deed piteouſly vnethes ſorow myight herte abyde body ſhe wold ful gladly haue deyed lordes fete ſawe neuer remedye ſhe beſieth wyth al might ye laſt ſeruice hym ye whiche ful vncouth dreſſe body beſt maner yt ſhe may ſhe wold ſhe hath neyther matere wherof tyme therto netheles maner ſhe maye ſhe waſſhith fete teres deuoutly wypeth hem kyſſeth hem wrappeth clothes beſt maner ſhe whan haue done dreſſed body hede loken lady yt ſhe wolde performe parte then̄e began al mekely wepe make ſorowe thenne ſhe ſeenge ſhe may noo lenger differ̄ ſett • th ſight vpō ye face ſone ſpekith hym maner ſwete ſone holde dede mi lappe ſee muſt depart bodili▪ harde ye departyng dede befor̄ likyng cōuerſacōn bitwene v liuynge amōge men euer wythout playnt offence though ſoo thou arte ſlayne wycked man haue ſerued ye truely thou ſorouful batayle thy fad er wolde helpe myghte wherfor̄ yu forſoke thyſelf loue mankynde thou woldeſt ayenbye ful harde painful dere bienge wherfore neuertheles gladde hele ſauacōn men thy paſſion deth full harde tormē ted wote wel thou dydeſt neuer ſyn̄e thou arte ſlayne wythout deſer te thrugh foule horryble dethe wherfor̄ dere ſone bodily feliſhip twyn̄ed▪ muſt nede departed fro ſoo ſhall berye whyder ſhall thy mooſt ſoroufull moder goo ſhall duelle dere ſone hou maye lyue wythout ſothly wolde gladly beryed wyth ſoo yt ſoo euer thou myght wyth ſythen maye beryed wyth bodily att leeſt ſhall beryed ghoſtly mynde wherfore ſhal berye thi body thy graue ſoule therfore cōmende leue ſwete ſone hou ſoroufull departynge therwyth grete habundance teeres ſhe wyſſhe moche better hede magdalayne dyde fete▪ then̄e ſhe wyped face kyſſed wounde hede ſudary ſo ſigned bleſſyd hym thenne togyder honouryng kyſſynge fete token vp beren hym graue lady berynge hede magdalayne fete mydyl part nyghe y• place croſſe ye ſpace ſtones caſt newe graue wher noo body beryed therin wyth reuerence kneling thei layed grete ſighinges ſobbinges wepynges ſoo beryed moder yeuen bleſſynge layden grete ſtone dore ye graue went way towarde cite ſaye joſeph felyſhyp joſeph gooynge ſpake lady ſayd lady praye goddis loue ye loue ſone maiſter ye voucheſauf come take herberough houſe wote well ye haue none hous owne wherfore takyth myn youre owne myn ben ſame maner nychodeme prayed ſyde ſhe louely enclinynge hē anſuerde ſayd ſhe cōmytted gouernaylle john▪wherfor̄ then̄e prayden john ſame ſuerde wolde lede mount syon theyr mayſter ſupped daye euē wyth diſcyples wold abyde wyth ſoo lowely ſaluenge lady worſyppyng ſepulture yeden forth waye ¶ done lady berienge jheſu caplm xlviii whan drewe nyght john ſpake lady ſayd▪it honeſt duelle lenger come cyte nyghte wherfore yf wyll goo hen torne agayne therwyth lady ryſeth vppe wyth hem knelynge bleſſed kyſſed ſepulture ſayd ſonne maye noo lenger ſtonde wyth y• recōmende thy fader then̄e lyftyng vppe eyen heuen teeres inwarde affeccōn ſayd fader almighty euerlaſtynge fader recōmende ſonne ſowle whyche leue wyth hym therwyth beganne goo alle theyr waye whan camen croſſe▪ ſhe kneled downe honoured croſſe ſayd made ſone ende precyous blode ſoo dyden thou mayſt thinke vnd er ſtonde ſhe firſt honoured croſſe ſhe firſt honoured ſo ne borne fro then token y• way towarde cyte oft waye ſhe loked agayn towarde ſone whan came myghte nomore ſee croſſe lady kneled honoured wepyng whā came nyghe cyte ladyes ſyſters hyled face maner morning wido w • yede befor̄ lady foloued bitwix mawdleyne john ſoo couerde face thē ne mawdleyne entree cyte deſirynge haue oure lady hous takynge waye▪ ladde thidward er e ſhe ſpake lady ſayd lady praye loue mayſter ye wol lete v goo hous bethanye maye beſte abyde ye knowe wel mayſter loued wel place came gladly ofte tymes therto hous wyth haue wherfore praye ye woll come • began wepe lady holdynge pee makinge ſygne john anſuere mawdaleyne prayenge hym ſame matere anſuerde ſayd ſemely goo mount syon namly ſoo anſuerde ſayd frendes wherfore come yu rather wyth place thenne ſayd mawdleyne john thou knoweſt well woll goo wyth whether ſoo euer ſhe gooth ſhall neuer leue whan camen cyte camen al ſydes maydens good •• one gooyng wyth ſorowyng comfortyng manere alſo good men wenten hadden grete cōpaſſion ſtyred wepyng ſaydē soothly daye done grete wronge prynces ſone lady god hath ſhewed grete token wonder bi hym auiſe hem haue done whan camen nygh place wolde reſte lady bowing lowely ladyes camen wyth thankyng hem ayeuwarde token leue makynge grete lamentacōn ſorowe then̄e lady mawdleyne ſyſters lady yeden hous john woyded wym̄en thāked hem ſhitt dore hem then̄e beynge ſoo hemſelf togid er lady lokynge aboute hous myſſyng loued ſone jhū grete ſorowe herte complayned her▪ ſaid john dere ſone ſoo highe ſpecyall affeccōn mawdleyne thy mayſter y• ſoo tenderly loued thou ſoo gladly ſeruedeſt hym dere ſyſters ſone soothly goon awaye fro v joye comforte lyghte eyen ye ſoothly goon wyth ſoo grete anguyſſh payne ye ſeen encreaſyth ſorowe paynes might helpe hym diſcyples forſoken fader almyghty wolde ſocour hym ſoone thoſe thynges ayenſt hym doon ye knowen haue ſeen euer ony theyf woors dooyng man ſoo ſoone dampned put ſoo pyteous dethe loo laſte nyght taken theyf erly morough brought juſtice▪ tyerce dāpned ſext croſſe hāged none deed beryed dere ſone bitter departyng this▪ ſo roufull mynde thy fouleſt horryble dethe thenne johan prayed ſtynte ſuche ſoroufull wordes ſeace wepynge comforted beſte manere y• coude ¶ thou alſo bi deuout ymaginacōn thou bodily preſent comforte lady felyſhyp prayenge hem ete ſomwhat yet ben faſtynge ſlepe trowe full lityll ſoo takynge theyr bleſſynge goo thy waye att tyme ¶ lady wyth dyden vpon ſaterdaye caplm xlix erly morough vpon ſaterday ſtoden ſayd hous ye yates ſperde lady john wym̄en named grete mornynge ſorowe hauynge mynde grete trybulacions anguyſſhes daye ſpekynge tymes lokynge manere done ben ouerlayed wyth grete myſcheyf ſorowe knowen none comforte ne none ſocoure therwyth herde one knocke yate then̄e dreden ſore thynge tyme dradden cauſe ſykerneſſe cōforte awaye neuertheles john went dore▪ vnd er ſtondyng peter tolde hem ſoo lady badde vndoo dore lete hym peter •• mynge 〈◊〉 grete ſhame wepynge ſobbynge ſaluted lady▪ nought ſpake therwyth began wepe myghte myſelf ſholde reaſon ſpeke preſence appere ſyghte men aſmoche left ſoo cowardly forſoke ſoo vntruely lorde loued ſomoche ſame maner ſmitynge hondes ſore wepynge accuſed reprehended hemſelf ſoo lefte lorde thenne lady comfortynge hem ſayd▪ oure gode lorde mayſter▪ true herdman goon fro v ben left fad er le chyldern hope truely y• ſhall ſoone hane hym agayn ye knowe well ſone benygne mercyful bleſſed may loued well therfore doubteth ſhall well • oucylied gladly ſhall foryeue treſpaſſes offence ſothly ſuffraūce fader malyce ayenſt hym ſo grete woodnes enmyes ſo ſtronge mighty ye myght haue ſocoured though ye abyde ſtyll wyth hym therfore dredeth ſhall well then̄e anſuerde peter ſayd ſothly ye ſaye ſoo ſawe lityll begynnyng wyth ſoo grete drede ſmyten porche cayphas houſe vnneth wende haue ſcaped deth therfore forſoke hym noo mynde att tyme wordes ſayd tyll loked mawdleyne aſked thoſe wordes ſaid tolde hym ſholde forſake hym tyme ſoo forth tolde wordes ſpoken hem ſpecyally y• tolde many thynges hem paſſion ſupper tyme made hē thurſday euen then̄e lady ſayd ſhe wold gladly proceſſe befell ſupper peter made ſygne john ſholde tell proceſſe john telleth al done ſayd peter tolde proceſſe paſſion deſyred ſo thiſe thynges done lorde jhū amonge hem tellen one another comyth mynde durynge awaye daye ſuche maner talkynges lord jhū lorde attentifly beſely mawdleine liſtned thoſe wordes moche lady ſaienge oft tymes ende proceſſe bleſſyd ſone jheſus namely whan ſhe mawdleyne herde makynge ſacrament yaaf hem ye forme brede owne body ete forme wyne blode drynke sothly trow yt wyth ſouerayn merueyle hertes melted likynge ſorowe ſoroufull likynge brekyng wepynge ſhedynge ſwete teres hye brennyng loue ſhewed man ſoueraynly excellent paſſige dede charyte paſſing ouer ſoo ſhortly ineditacōn tyme morouer take hede beholde hem daye grete ſorowe drede haue compaſſion hē yf thou canſt ſee lady al world prynceſſe holy chirche chyuetayns goddis peple ben ſoo drede ſorowe ſtoken hydde y• lityll hous knowinge maye doo hauynge comforte oonly comynge wordes dedes lorde jhū neuertheles lady ſtode alwaye ſadly reſtfull peaſyble herte ſhe euer certayne hope reſurreccōn ſone therfo • holy chyrche makyth mynde ſpecyall euery ſaterdaye dare ſtode on̄ly ye fayth lorde jhū god neuertheles ſhe myghte haue fully joye cauſe mynde harde dethe bytter paſſion whan ſon̄e gone downe leifful werche mary mawdleyne another mary yeden forth cyte bye mater able make oynements thei ſō done fridaye ſon̄e ſettelyng law boūde kepe ſabbot day fro y• ſon̄e reſte daye ſonne reſte goth hem takith brede bleſſith wyth holy hondes brekyth yeuyth hem then̄e ſhewyth hymſelf hem thus dooth wyth v euery day ghoſtly wolde bydde v dwell wyth v drawen wyth feruent deſires deuoute prayer
