cryſt apered bodily ooſt bothe ſy • ghtes liftynge vp right honde makynge croſſe toward kynge bleſſynge then̄e kynge wyth lowtyng hede honouryng preſence goddis mageſtec mekely wyth body dyde reuerence ſoo worthy bleſſinge erle ſawe ſelfe ſyghte knowynge y• kynges hert deſiryng kinge mighte partyner ſoo grete worthy ſyghte began goo towarde kynge fro place perauenture ſyde byneth longed aſtate kynge vnd er ſtondin ge • e entent ſaid maner stande leueryche ſtande thou ſeeſt ſee alſo bothe ſo joyefull ſighte ghoſtly comforted torned deuoute prayer ſwete wepynge teeres made ghoſtly dronken plēte goddis hous fed wyth ryuer ſouerayne joye ghoſtly lykynge ende maſſe ſoo bliſfully refeted wyth ghoſtly mete comyned togider forſayd heuenly ſiyght ſwete teres inwarde ſighynges▪ oft tymes brekinge ſpeches then̄e ſayd ſaynt edwarde dere leueryche praye charge hyghe mageſtee haue ſoo gracyonſly ſeen neuer whyle lyue thynge brought fourth comyn knowyng leeſt therby falle vaynglory pryde thrugh thoppinyon comyn peple ghoſtly dethe leeſt enuye myſbyleuynge men lette deſtroye true byleue wordes ther wherfore forſayd erle goon fro kynges courte juſpyracōn holy ghoſt byleue taughte ſoo kepte byddynge heſte lorde yet therwyth highe vertuous myracle ſholde fully vnknowen come came monaſtery wirceſtre confeſſion religyous man tolde forſayd myracle chargyng hym manere kynge charged prayed hym wolde wryte preuytee ſoo worthy viſyon put ſuche place mighte vnknowen hem then̄e liuynge myght knowen hem comyng ſo dyde holy mā erles prayer wrote thorder maner forſayd viſyon bylle layd amonge relyques cloſed cofre whiche cofre longe tyme ye kinges deth man̄es honde thrugh myghte god bileue founde open thenne bretherne place beſily ſerchynge reliques foūden forſayd bylle radde aſmoche wolde ſoo grete treſour worthy myracle ſholde hidde publyſſhed eeres peple openly ſoo kynge wolde tyme hydde ordynaūce god publyſſhed knowen ende kynges mekeneſſe therby hidde ſhold preued netheles therwyth open knowyng y• grete myracle y• faith true byleuinge men ſhold cōfermed ſtrēghthid worſhip lorde jhū ſpecial grace werchith ſuche myracles merueyles bleſſed ſacrament precyous body ſpecyall comfortynge true lyuers feruent ſtiringe loue amen ¶ alſo accordynge ſelfe purpoos fynde wrytynge longe lyfe ſaynt hughe biſſhop lyncolne firſte monke thorder charterhous pryour wytham whiche lyfe wrote chappellayn monke ſelfe order herde ſawe wrote amonge manere ſentence ſayenge befell vpon ſatirdaye forſayd byſſhop ſaynt hughe dwellynge maneer called bukedene ſange maſſe lady comyn cuſtome daye herde maſſe wyth deuoute clerke ſent hym ſpecyal reuelacōn god wherof wryten fayr proceſſe touchyng another matere whiche paſſen ouer purpoos tyme com̄ ſactynge byſſhop helde vp goddys body forme biede appered ſyghte forſayd clerke bitwyx preſtes holy hondes lorde god bodily lykenes paſſyng fayr lityll childe whiche ſyghte ſawe inwardly cō puncte noo wond er hiely ſtyred feruent deuocōn cōtynued tyme y• maſſe ſwete teres deuout prayer tyll came yt place thooſt ſholde lyft vp aboue chalyce departed thre whiche tyme efte ſawe ſelf lykenes forſayd jhū goddis ſone heuē fryng hymſelf ſa crefiſe fader man̄es hele ſaua cōn maſſe full ended ſelfe clerke ſpekynge wyth holy biſſhap preuyte tolde hym fyrſt reuelacy named y• fayr viſion goddis bodi declared therwyth th • de wyth ſhedyng teres maner cōcludynge ſayd thꝰ ſawe holy fader myn vn worthy eyen yt bleſſed ſyght whiche noo doubt yt ye ſeē alſo moche clerly lenger nere mot̄ worthily therwyth bothe byſſhop wyth ſwete teeres comynyng ghoſtly grete whyle togider counſeyle byſſhop biddyng kepe forſayd vyſion preuy clerke became religyoꝰ man holy liuynge went blyſſe euerlaſtynge amen touchynge ſeconde cauſe myracles merueyles ſhewedii cauſa mitac • rum bleſſed ſacramēt goddis body ſaye cōuerte hem ben myſbileue y• true byleue fuſte rede life ſaynt gregory pope worthy doctour maner ſentence ¶ matrone rome whiche euery ſondaye offred ſaynt gregory certain loues brede wherof made goddis body vpon ſondaye whan ſaynt gregory wolde haue comuned forſayd woman wyth one hem cōſe • rate made god dis body ſayeng comyn vſe holy chirche thyſe wordes body lorde jhū cryſte kepe euerlaſtyng lyf brake diſſolute laughter then̄e ſaynt gregory wythdrewe ſacrament fro kept ende maſſe peple aſked matrone ſhe lough then̄e ſhe ſaid cauſe thou calleſt goddis body brede haue made wyth hondes then̄e ſaynt gregory fell doune prayer god myſbyleue womā roſe vp fonde ſacrament torned lyknes finger fleſſhe blode thrugh woman fro miſbyleue torned true ſoo ſelf ſacrament prayer ſaynt gregory torned lykenes brede befor̄ ſhe comuned ſtyfly ſet true bileue bleſſed ſacrament alſo thru • worſhipp̄ highe gracyous auctour wercher herof lorde jheſus cryſte amen ſelf purpoos accordynge alſo fynde wryten forſayd life ſaynt hughe vpon tyme ſaynt hughe goynge thrugh fraunce inned tyme towne called joye came hym paryſſhe preeſte towne whiche olde man reuerent ſyight wond er lene grete penaūce doynge ſynnes ſuppoſed wherof folowith proceſſe whiche take ſhort wordes purpoſe y• ſelf preeſt tolde hymſelf maner whan yonge ſayd made preeſt neyther yeres ne maners accordynge worthy degree thrugh temptacōn ſtirynge fende felle grete dedely ſyn̄e whiche ſinne contynued without contrycōn confeſſyon horrible soo pollute body ſoule ghoſtly blynde ſeke fayth vſed boldly ſynge maſſe dradde treate receyue worthy ſacrament cryſtis precyous fleſſhe blood vpon daye maſſe tyme conſecracōn felle myude y• grete horryble ſyn̄e whyche ſolonge tyme contynued amonge wretched thoughtes blynde herte thought maner lorde whether precyous body fleſſhe blode lorde jhū called bryghtnes euerlaſtynge lyfe ghoſtly myrrour godhe de wythout wēme made treated receyued verely ſoo foule abhomynable ſyn̄er ſo hauyng ſuche vnthrifty thoughtes whan came tyme fraccy vſe broken thooſt two anone freſſhe blode ranne oute therof parte helde honde torned fleſſhe ouer al wete wyth reed blode therwyth ſeenge al aſtonyed abaſſhed well nyghe wytt ſoo loſte coūſeyle reaſon helde honde lete fall doune chalyce then̄e ſee yet wonderfull myracle ſaye wyne torned openly mannes ſyghte blode brede fleſſhe declarynge expreſſely forme ſothnes bleſſed ſacrament ferdermore ſayd whan ſawe maner lykenes abide ſtyll wythout ony tornynge chaūgynge durſt nomore touche hem pryuely hiled chalyce wyth patene paten wyth corporace maſſe doon peple awaye paſſed ſette chalyce wyth holy relyques yt yet day ben conteyned therin cōuenient place beſyde thaulter due reuerence kept went pope made hym confeſſion wyth ſothfaſt tellynge caas beforſayd ſynnes joyned penaūce due ſatyſfaccyon aſſoylled lete goo ſoo myracle publyſſhed knowen camen fro dyuers countrees moche folke ſee thoſe precyoꝰ relyques grete reuerence magnyfienge lorde alone werchith ſuche hye myracles merueyles then̄e thende forſayd preeſt prayed clerkes ſaynt hughe whiche tolde forſayde tale wolde alſo tell ſoo y• myght holpen anenſt god thorugh holy prayer whan ſo done ſuppoſynge wolde wyth grete deſyre haue goon ſee forſayd memeyles anſuerde maner ſentence worthily noted wchynge fayth holy ſacrament well ſayd name lorde lete hem haue hemſelf token myſbyle ue v thiſe thynges whether euery daye ſeen wyth trueſte inner ſyghte oure ſoule alle hooly fully heuenly ſacrifyce hauen merueyle pertyculers ymages yeft god ſayth nay lete hym goo ſee lityll ſmalle porcōns therof bodily eye ſeeth hole wyth inner ghoſtly eye whan thus ſayd yeuynge bleſſyng preſte goyng reprehēded meyne curyoſyte on̄ly ſtabled hem bileue alſo declared openly y• thoſe thynges faith techith v ſhold vnd er ſton de holde certaynly true bileuyng mē tho thī ge erthly lyghte reaſon ſheweth bodily ſyght thus lorde ſpecyall grace open myracles merueyles ſhewed bleſſed ſacrament drawith ſome folke oute myſbyleue ſtablyſſhed hem ſtrengthed true leue ſhewed u maners ¶ touchynge y• thirde cauſe ſhewenge myracles merueyles bleſſed ſacramēt open preyf grete vertues therof delyueraūce paynes ſauynge fro bodily myſcheyf ghoſtly saynt gregory tellyth dyalogues alſo omely vpon goſpel luke si quis venit ad longe tyme man taken enmyes ladde • ferre coūtre layed pryſon ſett harde bōdes longe tyme many dayes wyf y• de nomore ſuppoſed dede lete ſyng euery weke one maſſe offred ſacred ooſt ſoule▪and alſo oft maſſes ſoo done ſoule ſo tymes feters bondes looſed pryſon longe tyme whā delyuerde pryſon come home owne coūtree told wif grete merueyle y• certain dayes euery weke bondes loſed vndone▪and wif beſily accoūtyng notyng ſelf dayes vnd er ſtode wel knowledge oft ſhe lete offre ſacred ooſt hym ſoo oft looſed bōdes vndone then̄e forſayd ſaynt gregory concludeth ſentē ce wherfore dere bred er n herof certayn conſyderacōn takyth gadreth mynde ſacred ooſt offred v moche maye ourſelf vnbynde ghoſtly bonde herte fythen offred one man ſoo grete vertue myght looſe nother bōde body wherfore moche owyth euery preeſt loue ſynge hys maſſe oftymes dyſpoſe hym therto clene lyfe contrycion confeſſyon ¶ ſelfe purpoos alſo forſayd ſaynt gregory tellyth boke called dyalo gu vpon time whan biſſhop ſee towarde rome cam̄ vpon hym ſo grete tempeſt y• deſpeyre euer teſcape come londe ſhipmā y• lityll bote folowynge ſhyppe rope bote boūden ſhippe vyolence y• tempeſt broken ſodenly wyth ſelf bote ca • ſoo monge wawes ſee byſſhop ſawe nomore hym afterwarde whan biſſhoppis ſhippe af • many perylles dryuen londe certayn yle thyrd day went ſee ſyde beſyly lokyng whed er myght haue ſeen bote ſhypman beforſayd whā miyght ſee hē ony party y• ſee ſuppoſing y• ſhipman drowned dede hauyng grete ſorow hym • ete ſynge maſſe offre y• helful ſacrifyce goddis body thaſſoyling ſoule aftwarde ſayd ſhippe reſtored toke ſee towarde ytalye whan came y• hauen rome ſodenly foūde lyue forſayd ſhip man wende dede wherof gladde joyeful aſked hym maner myght lyue ſo many dayes ſo grete peryll y• ſee anſuerd tolde tymes flodes y• tēpeſt caſt vp doune aboue y• bote ful water vnd er laſt traueile faſtyng whan ſo ouercome nere dede wyſt neyther forſoth whed er ſlepte woke ſodenly hym thought one apered hym myddes ſee • ya ue hym brede ete whiche alſo ſone eten toke ſtrengthe ſoone ſhyppe came therby taken broughte londe whanne byſſhop aſked hym vnd er ſtode day whyche receyued ſayd brede▪and reuygored then̄e knew well ſelfe daye whiche lete preeſt ſynge offre ſacred ooſt forſayd yle ſoule thus ſhewyth oure lorde jhūs cryſt openly myracles merueyles ſouerayn vertue bleſſed ſacrament on̄ly helpynge ſauynge men alyue herbe for̄ſayd alſo charge looſynge vnbindynge ſoules hethen paſſed fyre purgatory ſelf ſaynt gregory tellyth forſaide boke playnly mōke ſyn̄e proper • e payne purgatory ſacred ooſt offred hym xxx dayes releaced delyuerde oute payne ¶ alſo nother ſoule delyuerde payne vertue bleſſed ſacrament offred al dayes weke may ſee openly preyf y• paſſynge profyte vertue ſpecyall maſſes done ſongen quycke dede ſelf ſaynt gregory ſayith holy ſacred ooſt ſyngulerly ſouerainly helpyth vn bynde ſoules fro ſynne mooſt pryncipally pleiſeth y• kyng heuen makyth hym ſoft v whan comith deme v ſoo offred wyth teeres compūccōn clennes herte hymſelf ryſynge fro deth ſhal neuer deye yet bleſſed ooſt v ſuffreth myſtetery oft offre hym thooſt paſſion ſoo oft maken newe v paſſōn vndindyng fro ſynne thus lorde jhūs full mercy ſhedyng v ſoueraynly endleſſe mercy makynge yeuynge mooſt precyous ghoſtly mete bleſſed body werchith dyuers maners ſayd merueyles myracles openly ſhewed excellent ſacrament yet contynueth pryuely wonderfully ther̄ voucheſauf hem true bileue loue dreden hym loue drede wanten many grete clerkes whiche leuen ſomoche vpon owne kindly reaſon prynciples phyloſophie mannes wyſdome grounded oonly kyndly reaſon man wol leue true faith taught holy chirche bleſſed ſacrament therefore fele ſothfaſt cō fortable effecte merueyles myracles ſayd neyther open ne preuy wchynge holy ſacrament wherfore moche folke ben deceiued party rather yeuē credence grete clerke techith acordyng kyndly reaſon holy chirche techith herof on̄ly byleue aboue reaſon maye noo man ſooner erre bileue ſacramentes holy chirche ſpecyally hyghe wonderfull ſacrament cryſt precyous fleſſh blood may grete clerkes haue grace true mekenes loue drede wherby leue owne wytt kindly reaſon ſubmytte hē lowely true byleue doctryne holy chyrche grace graūt v god ſpecially grete mercy thyſe laſte dayes ben ſemyth nyghe comynge antcryſt diſcyples whiche ſhall pryncipally foūde deſtroye true fayth bleſſed ſacrament grete clergy man̄es cūnynge merueyles myracles werchynge ſaynt gregory morale vpon worde cryſt goſpel ſpekynge antecryſt diſcyples ſayth ſentence ſhall ryſe vp fals cryſten men fals prophetes ſhal ſhew werke grete ſygnes wonder ſomoche ben goddis choſen folke yf maye ſhall brought errour sothly ſayth ſaynt gregory oure true marters▪werchen merueylles tyme ſuffren tormentes paynes then̄e ſaye comyng antcryſt diſcyples whan yeuen tormentes paynes ſhal alſo therwith werche miracle lete v thenne thinke haue mynde temptacyons mannes thought ſhall whanne meke marter ſubmyttith body tormentes neuertheles tormentour eyen werchyth myracles whoos vertue ſhall then̄e ſoo ſadly grounded byſeue ne ſhall meued thoughte tyme ſeeth y• tormenteth alſo therwyth ſygnes merueylles openly ſhyneth then̄e ſhal antecryſt highe worſhip merueilous werchyng harde ſharpe cruelte tormentyng thiſe ben wordes holy doctour ſaint gregori many moo ſpekynges wond er full myghte antcryſt diſcyples grete temptacōn ſhall tyme cryſten men lykely reaſon mooſte cōfort criſten byleue ſtant mooſt excellent ſacrament cryſtes body soo antcryſt diſcyples ſhall princypally werke deſtruccōn fyrſt tru bylene bleſſed ſacrament forſayd two maners ſay clergye euydence worldes cūnyng acordyng naturell reaſon many merueyles myracles werchyng falſe decepcōn fyrſte maner werchyng haue ſeen dayes diſcyples antecryſt ben called lollardes haue made moche deſcencyon diuyſion holy chirche put mani men errour bleſſed ſacramēt fals doctryne mayſter whiche thrugh grete clergye cūnynge phyloſophye deceyued yaue cred • ce doctryne aryſtotle ſtant onely naturell reyſon man thanne dyde doctryne holy chyrche true doctours therof touchynge precyous ſacrament aryſtotle techyth kyndely reaſon accordeth accydentes brede wyne ſay colour ſauour ſoo forth may ſubſtaūce brede wyne kynde doctryne holy chirche y• bleſſed ſacrament ſpecyal myracle god aboue kynde y• colour ſauonr accydentes brede wyne ben wythout kyndly ſub • ecte ſay without ſubſtaūce brede▪ wine conſecracōn aſmoche doctryne holy chirche ayēſt prynciples philoſophye naturell ſcyence therfore mayſter lollardes reproued ſcorned ſo errith himſelf made many erre touchyng bileue holieſt ſacrament whiche yeuen credence hym opinyon grete clergye true doctryne holy chyrche thus yet dayes hath antcryſt wrought fyrſt maner befor ſayd fals mayſter lollardes many diſcyples deſtruccōn true criſten byleue touchyng bleſſed ſacrament criſtis body many poyntes ayenſte holy chirche wythout ſeconde maner ſay werchynge merueylles myracles antecriſte hem ſoo grete power wyth reaſons alſo wroughte merueylles myracles lykely holy chirche true byleue ſpecially bleſſed ſacrament grete party deſtroyed vnſtablenes mooſt party peple notwithſtondyng grete merueyles myracles many ofte lorde hath ſhewed herbefore holy ſacrament ſayd ſtrength v ſtable v true byleue holy chirche hath taught v • ▪ whiche byleue reaſon ſhold ſoo ſadly 〈◊〉 ſentence apoſtle poul though came doun angel heuen taughte contrary ſholde yeue credence hym holde hym curſed ſooth maye noo true angel teche contrary bileue holy chirche therfor̄ ſoo dooth angell ſathanas god ben fals lollardes whiche haue neyther true drede perfyte loue oure lord jhū therfore fele ghoſtly ſwetnes heuenly mete precyous body ne likynge mynde merueylles ſhewed bleſſed ſacramente▪ thorugh grace ſtonden true byleue holy chyrche hath taught v ſouerayne holyeſt ſacrament wyth gooſtly lykynge ſowle haue oonly mynde grete merueylles myghty myracles wryten preched holy sacrament dyuerſe maners ſhewed beforſayd alſo conſider lorde jhūs vnſpeable goodnes ſhewed mankynde yeueth hym ſelf v euery daye bodily precious ſacrament concluſion mooſt ſpecyall mynde bleſſed lyf ſouerayne comforte helpe wretchid lyfe whyche full temptacōns ouerſette wyth many enmyes wherfore ſpedfull v contynuelly crye helpe ſonerayne vertue bleſſed ſacrament wordes holy chyrche ſyngeth ympne ſacrament thus thou helful ooſt openeſt door heuē bataylles enmyes oppreſſen ouerſeten v wherfore yeue v ſtrengthe wythſtondynge brynge v thy helpe ouercomyng alſo wythſtondynge temptacōns ouercomyng vice getynge vertues encreace feruent affeccōns lorde jhū full ende bleſſed lyfe wryten ¶ enprynted wynkin worth ¶ folowyth ſhorte deuoute prayer jhū cryſt body ſacrament aulter whiche oweth ſayd preſence holy ſacrament maſſe inwarde deuocōn heyle holyeſt body lorde jheſu cryſte art ſoothfaſtly conteyned mooſt excellent ſacrament knowlege lorde god wyth mouth loue wyth herte deſyre wyth inwarde affeccyon ſoule beſeche ſwete jhū thou vocheſauf thy ſouerayne goodnes daye ſoo benygnely gracyouſly vyſite ſike ſoule deſiryng receyue gooſtly heelfull ſacrifyce well grace ſoo may wyth gladneſſe fynde medecyne heele body ſoule vertue thy bleſſed preſence beholde lorde jhū wickydneſſe manyfolde neclygences grete vnkyndnes rather thy ſouerayne mercy endles godenes sothly thou arte holy lambe wythout wēme ſyn̄e yt day offred euerlaſtinge fader heuen redempcōn al ye worlde thou ſwetteſt man̄a angel mete▪ thou mooſt likynge ghoſtly drynke brynge inwarde mouth hony ſwete taaſt thy helfull preſence byadie feruour thy charyte quenche maner vyces shede plentee vertues encreace ye yeftes grace yeue heele body ſoule thy pleſynge god biſeche thou wolt ſoo gracyouſly bowe fro thy hye heuen come doune y• knytted joyned made one ſpiryte wyth y• worſhypfull ſacrament byſeche al myn enmyes put awaye fro ſtrengthe ſynnes foryeue wyckidnes excluded bleſſid preſence good purpoſe lorde yeue thou maners thou correcte amende al werkes dedes thou diſpoſe thy wyll wytte vnd er ſtondyng ſwete jhū made clere wyth newe lyghte grace myne affeccōn enflāmed wyth fyre thy loue myne hope cōforted ſtrengthed wyth bleſſid ſacrament ſoo lyf profyte euer amendynge better laſt fro wretchid worlde wyth bleſſed departyng maye come wyth lyf euerlaſtyng jhū lorde vertue grace thy lyfe bleſſed wythout endynge amen amen amen ¶ jhū lorde thy bleſſid lyfe helpe comforte wretchid lyfe amen ¶
